# pi-mcp Implementation Plan

> **For agentic workers:** REQUIRED SUB-SKILL: Use superpowers:subagent-driven-development (recommended) or superpowers:executing-plans to implement this plan task-by-task. Steps use checkbox (`- [ ]`) syntax for tracking.

**Goal:** Build pi-mcp, a Go MCP server that lets Claude Code delegate a TASK to pi's dynamic-workflow engine (multi-model fan-out), returning intermediate + final results.

**Architecture:** Stateless-credential stdio MCP server (go-sdk). Drives `pi -p --mode json` as background jobs (goroutine + persisted registry, cap 4), parses the JSONL stream + reads the live run file (journal[]) for intermediate results, isolates write mode in a git worktree. pi owns decomposition + model selection.

**Tech Stack:** Go, github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp, os/exec, git worktrees. Module: pi-mcp.

**Go-SDK API (verified):** VERIFIED (not assumed) against the official repo README and the official quick-start site, both fetched & indexed this session.
Sources:
- https://raw.githubusercontent.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/main/README.md (canonical greeter example, verbatim)
- https://go.sdk.modelcontextprotocol.io/quick_start/ (same example)
- https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp (package landing)

IMPORTANT ENV NOTE: `go` is NOT installed in this build environment (`go version` -> command not found; no module cache for the SDK under /root/go/pkg/mod). The plan's `go ...` commands are written to be run where Go (1.23+ recommended for generics + the SDK) IS installed. Task 1 includes a Go-presence check step.

Import path: `github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp`  (install: `go get github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk@latest`).

VERIFIED API (exact, from the README example):
1) Construct server:
   server := mcp.NewServer(&mcp.Implementation{Name: "pi-mcp", Version: "v0.1.0"}, nil)
   - NewServer(*mcp.Implementation, *mcp.ServerOptions) *mcp.Server. Implementation has Name and Version string fields. Pass nil ServerOptions for defaults.

2) Register a typed tool with the GENERIC top-level function mcp.AddTool (NOT a method on Server):
   mcp.AddTool(server, &mcp.Tool{Name: "greet", Description: "say hi"}, SayHi)
   - mcp.AddTool[In, Out any](s *mcp.Server, t *mcp.Tool, handler func(context.Context, *mcp.CallToolRequest, In) (*mcp.CallToolResult, Out, error))
   - The input/output JSON schemas are auto-derived from the In/Out struct types via reflection of `json:` + `jsonschema:` struct tags. No manual schema needed.

3) Handler signature (typed input + typed output) — VERBATIM from README:
   func SayHi(ctx context.Context, req *mcp.CallToolRequest, input Input) (*mcp.CallToolResult, Output, error) {
       return nil, Output{Greeting: "Hi " + input.Name}, nil
   }
   - Three returns: *mcp.CallToolResult (may be nil to let the SDK synthesize from the Output value), the typed Output struct, and error. Returning a non-nil error surfaces a tool error to the client.

4) Input/Output struct tag convention — VERBATIM from README:
   type Input struct {  Name string `json:"name" jsonschema:"the name of the person to greet"` }
   type Output struct { Greeting string `json:"greeting" jsonschema:"the greeting to tell to the user"` }
   - `json:"..."` controls the wire name; `jsonschema:"..."` provides the per-field description in the generated schema.

5) Run over stdio (subprocess transport, reads os.Stdin / writes os.Stdout):
   if err := server.Run(context.Background(), &mcp.StdioTransport{}); err != nil { log.Fatal(err) }
   - server.Run(ctx context.Context, t mcp.Transport) error. mcp.StdioTransport{} is the zero-value stdio transport. Run blocks until the client disconnects.

Full canonical program (package main): import "context","log","github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"; define Input/Output; define handler; in main() NewServer -> AddTool -> server.Run(ctx, &mcp.StdioTransport{}).

---

## Package API Contract (AUTHORITATIVE — supersedes any divergent signature in package tasks below)

This section resolves every cross-package seam. Where a package task below shows a different
signature, **this contract wins**. Package *internals* (helpers, tests, file layout) are
unchanged — only the seams listed here are pinned. Module path is `pi-mcp`; Go 1.23+.

### go-sdk pin (foundation Task 1 / Z1)

```
require github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk v1.0.0   // floor; any v1.x is API-stable
```

The SDK is at v1.x with a compatibility guarantee since v1.0.0. The server API
(`mcp.NewServer`, generic `mcp.AddTool`, `*mcp.Server.Run`, `mcp.StdioTransport`) and the
client API used by the e2e (`mcp.NewClient`, `(*mcp.Client).Connect`, `mcp.CommandTransport`,
`(*mcp.ClientSession).CallTool`, `mcp.CallToolParams`, `(*mcp.CallToolResult).StructuredContent`,
`mcp.TextContent`) are all present in v1.x. Replace every `@latest` with `@v1.0.0` (or a chosen
v1.x) so the build is reproducible. **Do not** use `@latest`.

Server handler signature (generic AddTool), unchanged from foundation:
```go
mcp.AddTool(m, &mcp.Tool{Name: "pi_workflow", Description: "..."},
    func(ctx context.Context, req *mcp.CallToolRequest, in model.WorkflowInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, model.WorkflowOutput, error) { ... })
```

---

### internal/config — error consts (foundation Task 5 owns the file)

`internal/config/config.go` is the SINGLE owner of these string consts (already in Task 5).
Every other package MUST reference these and never re-declare them, and never use string
literals for codes:

```go
const (
    ErrModelRoutingError     = "MODEL_ROUTING_ERROR"
    ErrAgentTimeout          = "AGENT_TIMEOUT"
    ErrAgentExecutionError   = "AGENT_EXECUTION_ERROR"
    ErrWorkflowAborted       = "WORKFLOW_ABORTED"
    ErrAgentLimitExceeded    = "AGENT_LIMIT_EXCEEDED"
    ErrTokenBudgetExhausted  = "TOKEN_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED"
    ErrScriptValidationError = "SCRIPT_VALIDATION_ERROR"
    ErrSchemaNoncompliance   = "SCHEMA_NONCOMPLIANCE"
    ErrPersistenceError      = "PERSISTENCE_ERROR"
    ErrUnknown               = "UNKNOWN"
    ErrNotAGitRepo           = "NOT_A_GIT_REPO"   // worktree.New uses THIS, not model.ErrNotAGitRepo
    ErrNoWorkflowRun         = "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN"
)
```

`model.ErrNotAGitRepo` does **not** exist and must not be introduced. `worktree.New` returns
`errors.New(config.ErrNotAGitRepo)`. `jobs.finish` populates `JobRecord.ErrorCode` with
`config.ErrAgentExecutionError` / `config.ErrWorkflowAborted` (never literals).

### internal/model — ListItem + tool I/O (foundation Task 3 owns the file)

Unchanged from foundation Task 3. The two seam types other packages reach for:

```go
type ListItem struct {
    RunID        string         `json:"runId"`
    WorkflowName string         `json:"workflowName"`
    Status       string         `json:"status"`
    AgentCount   int            `json:"agentCount"`
    ByModel      map[string]int `json:"by_model"`
    Cost         *float64       `json:"cost,omitempty"`
    DurationMs   *int64         `json:"durationMs,omitempty"`
    CompletedAt  *time.Time     `json:"completedAt,omitempty"`
}

type WriteInfo struct {
    Branch       string   `json:"branch"`
    WorktreePath string   `json:"worktree_path"`
    DiffStat     string   `json:"diff_stat"`
    FilesChanged []string `json:"files_changed"`
}
```

`model.JobRecord` is the persisted record; the **ErrorMessage** field is the primary §9
failure text (set by jobs from the parser workflow `isError` content). NO new model fields
are added by this contract. (DiffStat/files surface through the worktree adapter at status
time, not through JobRecord.)

---

### internal/parser — stream parse (package P owns it; signature pinned)

```go
package parser

type Result struct {
    SessionID     string          // first session event id (== Run.SessionID)
    WorkflowFound bool            // true iff tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow") seen
    IsError       bool            // that event's isError
    RawText       string          // content[0].text of the workflow tool_execution_end
    Result        json.RawMessage // fenced ```json``` block (or raw text JSON-wrapped); nil if none
}

func ParseStream(ctx context.Context, r io.Reader) (Result, error) // err only on fatal read
```

The Launcher adapter (internal/app) consumes `Result.SessionID` for correlation and
`Result.WorkflowFound`/`IsError`/`RawText`/`Result` to decide success and the §9 #1 failure
text. `ParseStream` must be tolerant of an `io.Reader` that is being drained concurrently
with `proc.Wait()`.

---

### internal/runner — spawn + prompt (package N owns it; signatures pinned)

```go
package runner

// RenderPrompt builds the single positional prompt: forcing template + §5.4 contract
// skeleton (by mode) + task + optional context. mode is "read"|"write".
func RenderPrompt(mode, task, context string) (string, error)

func BuildArgv(prompt string, noContextFiles bool) []string

type SpawnConfig struct {
    Prompt         string    // already-rendered (RenderPrompt output)
    NoContextFiles bool
    CWD            string    // project (read) or worktree (write)
    Stderr         io.Writer // required; diagnostic only; runner never logs it
}

type Process struct {
    Stdout io.ReadCloser // pi JSONL stream; read to EOF then Wait
    // cmd, devnull unexported
}

func Spawn(ctx context.Context, cfg SpawnConfig) (*Process, error) // stdin=/dev/null, env=os.Environ(), cwd=cfg.CWD
func (p *Process) Wait() error // exit error; nil on exit 0
func (p *Process) PID() int    // 0 before start
```

Cancellation: cancel the `ctx` passed to `Spawn` → SIGKILL. The runner makes no
success/failure decision; the parser + runstore do.

---

### internal/runstore — read funcs (package R owns it; ADD the 3 new funcs)

KEEP the existing exported funcs verbatim:
```go
func ReadRun(path string) (*model.Run, error)                  // .bak fallback on corrupt
func ModelHistogram(r *model.Run) map[string]int
func Intermediates(r *model.Run, maxInlineBytes int) []model.IntermediateResult
func AuthoritativeResult(r *model.Run) (json.RawMessage, bool) // completed only
func Metadata(r *model.Run) model.StatusMetadata
func ListRuns(dir string, limit int) (model.ListOutput, error) // excl .bak/.tmp, sorted
```

ADD three new exported funcs (new file `internal/runstore/lookup.go`) — these are the
production seam the app adapters wrap. `runsDir` is the full
`<cwd|worktree>/.pi/workflows/runs` directory:

```go
package runstore

import (
    "encoding/json"
    "errors"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"

    "pi-mcp/internal/config"
    "pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// ErrRunNotFound is returned (wrapped) by Load when the run file does not exist
// (blind window / not-yet-created). mcpserver maps its own sentinel onto errors.Is(this).
var ErrRunNotFound = errors.New("runstore: run file not found")

// RunIDForSession scans runsDir for a run file whose sessionId == sessionID and
// returns its runId. ok=false if none matches yet (blind window). Reuses ReadRun
// (so .bak fallback + decode rules are shared). Never errors: a missing/unreadable
// dir yields ("", false).
func RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID string) (runID string, ok bool) {
    entries, err := os.ReadDir(runsDir)
    if err != nil {
        return "", false
    }
    for _, e := range entries {
        n := e.Name()
        if e.IsDir() || !hasJSONSuffix(n) {
            continue
        }
        r, derr := ReadRun(filepath.Join(runsDir, n))
        if derr != nil {
            continue
        }
        if r.SessionID == sessionID && sessionID != "" {
            return r.RunID, true
        }
    }
    return "", false
}

// Load reads <runsDir>/<runID>.json into a model.Run. A missing file is reported
// as a wrapped ErrRunNotFound (so callers do errors.Is(err, runstore.ErrRunNotFound)).
func Load(runsDir, runID string) (*model.Run, error) {
    path := filepath.Join(runsDir, runID+".json")
    if _, err := os.Stat(path); errors.Is(err, os.ErrNotExist) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("load %s: %w", runID, ErrRunNotFound)
    }
    return ReadRun(path)
}

// ListItems is the cwd-relative convenience wrapper over ListRuns: it resolves the
// runs dir as <cwd>/config.RunsDirRel and returns the rows. (mcpserver.RunStore seam.)
func ListItems(cwd string, limit int) ([]model.ListItem, error) {
    out, err := ListRuns(filepath.Join(cwd, config.RunsDirRel), limit)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    return out.Runs, nil
}
```
(`hasJSONSuffix` = `strings.HasSuffix(n,".json") && !strings.HasSuffix(n,".bak") && !strings.HasSuffix(n,".tmp")`;
add `fmt`/`strings` imports. If ListRuns already lives in `list.go`, these can go there instead.)

---

### internal/worktree — manager (package W owns it; ONE fix)

Signatures stay exactly as the W package PROVIDES them. The ONLY change: `New` returns
`config.ErrNotAGitRepo` (W3 currently writes `model.ErrNotAGitRepo`, which does not exist).

```go
package worktree

type Manager struct{ repoCWD string } // unexported field

func New(ctx context.Context, cwd string) (*Manager, error) // not-a-repo => errors.New(config.ErrNotAGitRepo)

type Handle struct {
    JobID        string
    Path         string // absolute worktree path OUTSIDE repoCWD
    Branch       string // pi-mcp/job-<jobId>
    BaseCommit   string // HEAD sha branch cut from
    DirtyWarning string // warn+proceed
}

func (m *Manager) Create(ctx context.Context, jobID string) (*Handle, error)
func (m *Manager) Diff(ctx context.Context, h *Handle) (diffStat string, filesChanged []string, err error)
func (m *Manager) WriteInfo(ctx context.Context, h *Handle) (model.WriteInfo, error)
func (m *Manager) Prune(ctx context.Context, h *Handle) error
func (m *Manager) PruneOrphans(ctx context.Context) ([]string, error)
```

`Create` produces `RunsDir = <Handle.Path>/.pi/workflows/runs` for the job (assembled by the
caller via `filepath.Join(h.Path, config.RunsDirRel)`). `Diff`/`WriteInfo` compare the worktree
(index+worktree) vs `h.BaseCommit`; the caller must `git add -A` the worktree before WriteInfo
to surface new files (the app status adapter does this).

---

### internal/jobs — Registry seam (package J owns internals; RECONCILE the public seam)

Pin ONE constructor and ONE method set. The mcpserver consumer (via the app adapter) needs
`Submit / Lookup / LookupByRun / Cancel(→JobRecord)`; package J today has
`Launch / Get / Cancel(→CancelResult) / StatusOf / Reconcile`. Reconcile as follows.

**Spec — add Task + Context (blocker #3):**
```go
type Spec struct {
    Mode     model.JobMode
    CWD      string
    RunsDir  string
    Task     string // NEW: the user task (rendered into the forcing prompt by the Launcher)
    Context  string // NEW: optional extra context
    Worktree string // write mode only
    Branch   string // write mode only
}
```
`NewJob(spec)` copies Task/Context onto the *Job (kept in-memory only; NOT persisted to
JobRecord — they may contain secrets, spec §1). The Launcher reads them off the Spec it is
handed.

**Dependency interfaces (unchanged) + LaunchHandle:**
```go
type Launcher interface {
    // Launch starts pi; returns once the PID is known (does NOT block to completion).
    // sessionCh receives the first session id exactly once (closed if none). wait blocks
    // until exit; a non-nil error means the workflow failed. The error string, when present,
    // is the §9 #1 failure text (parser workflow isError content) — store it on the record.
    Launch(ctx context.Context, spec Spec) (pid int, sessionCh <-chan string, wait func() error, err error)
}
type Correlator interface {
    RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID string) (runID string, ok bool)
}
type Pruner interface {
    Prune(worktreePath, branch string) error
}
```
(There is no separate `LaunchHandle` type; the 4-tuple return IS the launch handle. Keep it.)

**Constructor (blocker #2) — PIN `NewRegistry`, DROP `jobs.New`:**
```go
type Config struct {
    Cap          int
    PersistPath  string
    WorktreeRoot string
    Now          func() time.Time
}
func NewRegistry(cfg Config, l Launcher, c Correlator, p Pruner) *Registry
```
The Z-seam's `jobs.New(ctx, jobs.Options{...})` is REMOVED. Dependency injection happens at
`NewRegistry`: the app package builds the real Launcher/Correlator/Pruner and passes them in.
There is no `jobs.Options`, no `jobs.New`.

**Registry methods (blocker #1) — RENAME + ADD, keep lifecycle:**
```go
// Submit replaces Launch. Same body; renamed. Ignores ctx for admission (kept for the
// interface), spawns its own per-job context internally as today.
func (r *Registry) Submit(ctx context.Context, spec Spec) (model.JobRecord, error)

// Lookup replaces the test-only Get for the consumer seam (keep Get as an alias if J's
// own tests use it, or rename Get→Lookup and update J9/J10 tests).
func (r *Registry) Lookup(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, bool)

// LookupByRun finds a job by (runID, cwd). It matches a record whose RunID==runID AND
// (CWD==cwd OR WorktreePath==cwd) — the pi_status runId path passes the launch cwd for read
// jobs and the worktree_path for write jobs (spec §5.2/§5.3).
func (r *Registry) LookupByRun(runID, cwd string) (model.JobRecord, bool)

// Cancel now returns model.JobRecord (was CancelResult). Body unchanged except the return:
// build the record snapshot instead of CancelResult{}. Delete the CancelResult type.
func (r *Registry) Cancel(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, error)

// Lifecycle — KEEP:
func (r *Registry) Reconcile(ctx context.Context) (int, error) // was Reconcile() error; return count reconciled
func (r *Registry) Close() error                               // NEW: cancels in-flight + final flush; idempotent
func (r *Registry) StatusOf(jobID string, sameSession bool) model.JobStatus // keep (internal liveness)
```

Notes for J executor:
- `Submit` is the J9 `Launch` body verbatim, renamed; the `ctx` param is accepted and ignored
  (or used as the parent for the per-job context).
- `Reconcile() error` → `Reconcile(ctx context.Context) (int, error)`: return
  `len(records)` (records loaded/reconciled). Tests in J13 adjust the call to `r.Reconcile(context.Background())`
  and read the count (or `_`).
- `Cancel` returns the live snapshot: replace `return CancelResult{JobID: jobID, Status: st}, nil`
  with `return j.snapshot(), nil` (and the queued/running branches likewise). Delete `CancelResult`.
- `Close()`: cancel every running job's `j.cancel` (no status change — kill is best-effort),
  then `flushUnlocked()`. The app `defer reg.Close()` calls it; idempotent.
- The real Launcher's `wait()` error string is the parser §9-#1 text; `finish` writes it to
  `JobRecord.ErrorMessage` (already does) and the ErrorCode is derived by the Launcher/finish
  (see §9 below).

---

### internal/mcpserver — Server + ports (package M owns it; KEEP M's shape, drop Z's wrong seam)

The M-package shape is AUTHORITATIVE; the Z assumption
`mcpserver.Register(s *mcp.Server, reg *jobs.Registry)` is WRONG and removed.

```go
package mcpserver

type JobSpec struct {
    Task    string
    Mode    model.JobMode
    CWD     string // validated absolute/exists/symlink-resolved
    Context string
}

type JobsService interface {
    Submit(ctx context.Context, spec JobSpec) (model.JobRecord, error)
    Lookup(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, bool)
    LookupByRun(runID, cwd string) (model.JobRecord, bool)
    Cancel(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, error)
}

type RunStore interface {
    Load(runsDir, runID string) (*model.Run, error) // missing => wrapped ErrRunNotFound
    ListItems(cwd string, limit int) ([]model.ListItem, error)
}

// ErrRunNotFound is the sentinel handlers test with errors.Is. The runstore adapter
// in internal/app maps runstore.ErrRunNotFound onto this.
var ErrRunNotFound = errors.New("run file not found")

type Server struct { /* jobs, store, now, waitCap, pollInterval, pidAlive */ }

func New(jobs JobsService, store RunStore) *Server
func (s *Server) Register(m *mcp.Server)            // AddTool x4 (pi_workflow/status/list/cancel)
func (s *Server) RegisteredToolNames() []string
```

`mcpserver` imports NEITHER `jobs` NOR `runstore` — only `model`/`config`/`mcp`. The two
interfaces are its entire downstream surface. The `JobSpec→jobs.Spec` mapping is NOT done in
mcpserver; it is done in the app adapter (see below): mcpserver hands a `mcpserver.JobSpec`
to `JobsService.Submit`, and the app adapter translates it (adding worktree orchestration).

§9 fix in `handler_status.go::failureMessage` (blocker #9) — it currently starts at
`agents[].error`; it MUST start at the record's ErrorMessage. The handler already has the
JobRecord via `resolveTarget`; thread `tgt.errorMessage`/`tgt.errorCode` (add those two fields
to `resolved`, populated from the looked-up record) into `buildStatus`:
```go
// order: (#1) JobRecord.ErrorMessage (parser workflow isError text) →
//        (#2) run agents[].error → (#3) run logs[0] verbatim → generic.
func failureMessage(recMsg string, run *model.Run) string {
    if recMsg != "" {
        return recMsg
    }
    for _, a := range run.Agents {
        if a.Status == "error" && a.Error != nil && *a.Error != "" {
            return *a.Error
        }
    }
    if len(run.Logs) > 0 {
        return run.Logs[0]
    }
    return config.ErrUnknown
}
```
ErrorCode derivation (for the mapped status): `WORKFLOW_ABORTED → aborted`, any other code →
`failed`. The disk→MCP status map already handles aborted/failed; the code only refines the
surfaced `error` string. The write-info DiffStat/FilesChanged are populated by the app status
adapter via a `WriteInfo(runsDir/worktree)` hook (see app), not by mcpserver directly — keep
mcpserver's behavior of leaving them empty and let the adapter enrich. (Simplest: the status
adapter's `RunStore` is unchanged; WriteInfo enrichment is done inside the JobsService adapter
exposing a `WriteInfoFor(rec)` the handler calls — OR, to avoid widening the interface, the
app builds WriteInfo at status time by having the worktree-backed status enrichment live in a
3rd seam. See integration task "WriteInfo wiring" for the pinned approach: widen RunStore is
NOT done; instead JobsService gains an optional `WriteInfoFor`.)

**Pinned WriteInfo approach (avoids interface churn):** add ONE method to `JobsService`:
```go
// WriteInfoFor returns the live diff for a write job (branch/worktree/diff_stat/files_changed).
// ok=false for read jobs or when the worktree is gone. mcpserver calls it in buildStatus when
// tgt.mode==ModeWrite && tgt.hasJob, replacing the empty WriteInfo block.
WriteInfoFor(jobID string) (model.WriteInfo, bool)
```
The fake in M2 implements it returning `{}, false` by default; M9's `TestStatus_WriteInfoPopulated`
sets `f.writeInfo[jobID]` so Branch/WorktreePath assert. This is the only mcpserver interface
addition; it keeps DiffStat/FilesChanged real in production.

---

### internal/app — the wiring seam + the production adapters (package Z owns it; REWRITE adapters)

`internal/app` is the only place that imports runner, runstore, worktree, jobs, AND mcpserver.
It constructs the three jobs deps + the two mcpserver deps and passes BOTH into
`mcpserver.New`. `main.go` stays a 3-line delegate to `app.Run`.

```go
package app

import (
    "context"
    "errors"
    "fmt"
    "log"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"

    "github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

    "pi-mcp/internal/config"
    "pi-mcp/internal/jobs"
    "pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver"
    "pi-mcp/internal/model"
    "pi-mcp/internal/parser"
    "pi-mcp/internal/runner"
    "pi-mcp/internal/runstore"
    "pi-mcp/internal/worktree"
)

// ---------- Run (entrypoint) ----------

type Deps struct {
    Logger      *log.Logger
    PersistPath string // default: <XDG_STATE>/pi-mcp/registry.json
    WorktreeRoot string // default: <XDG_STATE> (worktree.go resolves the subdir)
    // unexported test seams (nil in production; fill() installs reals):
    buildRegistry func(d Deps) (*jobs.Registry, error)
    newServer     func() *mcp.Server
    serve         func(ctx context.Context, m *mcp.Server) error
}

// Run: build registry (with real adapters) -> Reconcile (graceful) -> build mcpserver
// (jobs adapter + runstore adapter) -> Register -> serve over stdio.
func Run(ctx context.Context, d Deps) error {
    d = fill(d)
    reg, err := d.buildRegistry(d)
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("build registry: %w", err)
    }
    defer func() { _ = reg.Close() }()

    if n, rerr := reg.Reconcile(ctx); rerr != nil {
        d.Logger.Printf("startup reconcile error: %v (continuing)", rerr)
    } else {
        d.Logger.Printf("startup reconciled %d job record(s)", n)
    }

    js := &jobsAdapter{reg: reg, root: d.WorktreeRoot, log: d.Logger}
    rs := &runStoreAdapter{}
    srv := mcpserver.New(js, rs)

    m := d.newServer()
    srv.Register(m)
    d.Logger.Printf("serving pi-mcp v0.1.0 over stdio (tools=%v)", srv.RegisteredToolNames())
    if err := d.serve(ctx, m); err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("serve: %w", err)
    }
    return nil
}

// ---------- runStoreAdapter: mcpserver.RunStore over runstore ----------

type runStoreAdapter struct{}

func (runStoreAdapter) Load(runsDir, runID string) (*model.Run, error) {
    r, err := runstore.Load(runsDir, runID)
    if errors.Is(err, runstore.ErrRunNotFound) {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("%w", mcpserver.ErrRunNotFound) // map sentinel
    }
    return r, err
}
func (runStoreAdapter) ListItems(cwd string, limit int) ([]model.ListItem, error) {
    return runstore.ListItems(cwd, limit)
}

// ---------- jobsAdapter: mcpserver.JobsService over *jobs.Registry (+ worktree create-on-submit) ----------

type jobsAdapter struct {
    reg  *jobs.Registry
    root string
    log  *log.Logger
}

// Submit does create-on-submit worktree orchestration for write mode (blocker #6), then
// builds the jobs.Spec and delegates to the registry.
func (a *jobsAdapter) Submit(ctx context.Context, in mcpserver.JobSpec) (model.JobRecord, error) {
    spec := jobs.Spec{
        Mode:    in.Mode,
        CWD:     in.CWD,
        Task:    in.Task,
        Context: in.Context,
        RunsDir: filepath.Join(in.CWD, config.RunsDirRel),
    }
    if in.Mode == model.ModeWrite {
        mgr, err := worktree.New(ctx, in.CWD) // fail-before-spawn: config.ErrNotAGitRepo
        if err != nil {
            return model.JobRecord{}, err
        }
        // jobId is minted by the registry; but the branch name needs the id up front.
        // Resolution: Create takes a caller-supplied id. Mint here and pass to both.
        id := newJobID()
        h, err := mgr.Create(ctx, id)
        if err != nil {
            return model.JobRecord{}, err
        }
        spec.PreassignedID = id // see Spec note below
        spec.Worktree = h.Path
        spec.Branch = h.Branch
        spec.CWD = h.Path
        spec.RunsDir = filepath.Join(h.Path, config.RunsDirRel)
        a.remember(id, mgr, h) // for WriteInfoFor + cancel-prune
    }
    return a.reg.Submit(ctx, spec)
}

func (a *jobsAdapter) Lookup(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, bool)        { return a.reg.Lookup(jobID) }
func (a *jobsAdapter) LookupByRun(runID, cwd string) (model.JobRecord, bool) { return a.reg.LookupByRun(runID, cwd) }
func (a *jobsAdapter) Cancel(jobID string) (model.JobRecord, error)       { return a.reg.Cancel(jobID) }

// WriteInfoFor enriches pi_status for write jobs (blocker #6 WriteInfo). Looks up the
// remembered manager+handle, git-adds the worktree, and returns the diff.
func (a *jobsAdapter) WriteInfoFor(jobID string) (model.WriteInfo, bool) {
    e, ok := a.handle(jobID)
    if !ok {
        return model.WriteInfo{}, false
    }
    wi, err := e.mgr.WriteInfo(context.Background(), e.h) // WriteInfo stages internally or app stages first
    if err != nil {
        return model.WriteInfo{}, false
    }
    return wi, true
}
```

**jobs.Spec gets ONE more field for create-on-submit** so the worktree branch and the jobId
match (the branch is `pi-mcp/job-<jobId>`):
```go
type Spec struct {
    // ...Mode, CWD, RunsDir, Task, Context, Worktree, Branch as above...
    PreassignedID string // NEW: when non-empty, NewJob uses this as JobID instead of minting
}
```
`NewJob`: `id := spec.PreassignedID; if id == "" { id = uuid.NewString() }`. The app mints the
id (via `newJobID()` = `uuid.NewString()` in app, OR expose `jobs.NewID()`) so the worktree
branch created BEFORE submit matches the registry record. (Alternative if J prefers no Spec
field: jobsAdapter calls a tiny `jobs.NewID()` helper and passes it as `PreassignedID`.)

**Pruner seam (blocker #7):** jobs calls `Pruner.Prune(worktreePath, branch)` (free-form
args). The app provides a worktree-backed pruner that rebuilds a minimal Handle:
```go
type worktreePruner struct{ root string } // root = repo cwd is unknown at prune time → use a free func

// Because jobs holds only (worktreePath, branch), the adapter reconstructs a Handle and
// prunes. worktree.Prune needs a *Manager bound to a repo cwd, which is gone post-cancel.
// PIN: add a free function to the worktree package:
//   func Prune(ctx context.Context, worktreePath, branch string) error
// implemented by running `git -C <parent-of-worktree> worktree remove --force <path>` is not
// reliable; instead derive the main repo from `git -C <worktreePath> rev-parse
// --git-common-dir` then operate from there. The app pruner is then:
func (worktreePruner) Prune(worktreePath, branch string) error {
    return worktree.Prune(context.Background(), worktreePath, branch)
}
```
**worktree package ADDS one free function** (alongside the Manager methods):
```go
// Prune removes a single worktree+branch given only its path+branch (no Manager needed).
// It resolves the owning repo via `git -C <worktreePath> rev-parse --git-common-dir`,
// then runs worktree remove --force / branch -D / worktree prune from there. Idempotent.
func Prune(ctx context.Context, worktreePath, branch string) error
```
This is the chosen reconciliation for blocker #7 (free-func over app-rebuilds-Handle, because
the Manager needs a live repo cwd the registry does not store).

**Launcher (blocker #4a) — the production adapter, defined in internal/app:**
```go
type realLauncher struct{}

func (realLauncher) Launch(ctx context.Context, spec jobs.Spec) (int, <-chan string, func() error, error) {
    prompt, err := runner.RenderPrompt(string(spec.Mode), spec.Task, spec.Context)
    if err != nil {
        return 0, nil, nil, err
    }
    proc, err := runner.Spawn(ctx, runner.SpawnConfig{
        Prompt:         prompt,
        NoContextFiles: config.DefaultNoContextFiles,
        CWD:            spec.CWD,
        Stderr:         io.Discard, // never log stdout/stderr (spec §1)
    })
    if err != nil {
        return 0, nil, nil, err
    }
    sessionCh := make(chan string, 1)
    parseDone := make(chan parser.Result, 1)
    go func() {
        res, _ := parser.ParseStream(ctx, proc.Stdout) // tolerant; err only on fatal read
        if res.SessionID != "" {
            select { case sessionCh <- res.SessionID: default: }
        }
        close(sessionCh)
        parseDone <- res
    }()
    wait := func() error {
        werr := proc.Wait()
        res := <-parseDone
        // Success = a workflow tool_execution_end with isError:false.
        if !res.WorkflowFound {
            return errors.New(config.ErrNoWorkflowRun)
        }
        if res.IsError {
            return errors.New(rawErrText(res)) // §9 #1 text → stored on JobRecord.ErrorMessage
        }
        if werr != nil {
            return werr
        }
        return nil
    }
    return proc.PID(), sessionCh, wait, nil
}
```
Note: `sessionCh` must be pushed BEFORE `wait()` is called for correlation; the goroutine
streams concurrently while the registry's correlate goroutine reads `sessionCh`. The first
`session.id` is emitted early (before the run file exists — blind window), satisfying §3.

**Correlator (blocker #4b):**
```go
type realCorrelator struct{}
func (realCorrelator) RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID string) (string, bool) {
    return runstore.RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID)
}
```

**buildRegistryReal (blocker #2 wiring):**
```go
func buildRegistryReal(d Deps) (*jobs.Registry, error) {
    return jobs.NewRegistry(jobs.Config{
        Cap:          config.DefaultConcurrencyCap,
        PersistPath:  d.PersistPath,
        WorktreeRoot: d.WorktreeRoot,
    }, realLauncher{}, realCorrelator{}, worktreePruner{}), nil
}
```

    }
}
```

## Foundation (types, config, errors)

# pi-mcp — FOUNDATION tasks (Task 0 layer: module + internal/model + internal/config)

> Goal: stand up the Go module, directory layout, and the two zero-dependency leaf packages (`internal/model`, `internal/config`) that EVERY downstream package compiles against. After this layer, parser/runstore/worktree/runner/jobs/mcpserver can all be drafted in parallel against a stable type contract.
>
> Style: bite-sized TDD steps (2-5 min each). Each code step shows COMPLETE Go source. Run the exact `go` command shown; expected output is given. Commit at the marked steps. NOTE: `go` must be installed (Go 1.23+). This environment does not have it — run these where Go is available.

## Task 2 — internal/model: write the failing test first (TDD)

We pin the exact JSON shapes from spec §7 and the canonical fixture `docs/research/fixtures/sample-run.json`. Optionals are POINTERS; arbitrary workflow output is `json.RawMessage`; `Cost` is `float64` read verbatim.

**2a. Write the test FIRST.** Create `internal/model/model_test.go`:
```go
package model

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"os"
	"testing"
)

func TestUnmarshalSampleRun(t *testing.T) {
	b, err := os.ReadFile("../../docs/research/fixtures/sample-run.json")
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("read fixture: %v", err)
	}
	var r Run
	if err := json.Unmarshal(b, &r); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unmarshal Run: %v", err)
	}
	if r.RunID != "mq40rdpt-yij9hj" {
		t.Errorf("RunID = %q", r.RunID)
	}
	if r.SessionID != "019ea2fe-db76-7e31-85ad-9718d3fbc23a" {
		t.Errorf("SessionID = %q", r.SessionID)
	}
	if r.Status != "completed" {
		t.Errorf("Status = %q", r.Status)
	}
	if r.CurrentPhase == nil || *r.CurrentPhase != "Final" {
		t.Errorf("CurrentPhase = %v", r.CurrentPhase)
	}
	if len(r.Agents) != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("len(Agents) = %d", len(r.Agents))
	}
	if len(r.Journal) != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("len(Journal) = %d", len(r.Journal))
	}
	// journal is in completion order, NOT array position: index 0,2,1,3
	if r.Journal[1].Index != 2 {
		t.Errorf("Journal[1].Index = %d, want 2 (out-of-order)", r.Journal[1].Index)
	}
	// agents[].id == callIndex+1
	a0 := r.Agents[0]
	if a0.CallIndex != 0 || a0.ID != 1 {
		t.Errorf("agent0 callIndex/id = %d/%d", a0.CallIndex, a0.ID)
	}
	if a0.Model != "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash" {
		t.Errorf("agent0 model = %q", a0.Model)
	}
	// token usage: cost is verbatim float64, total present
	if r.TokenUsage == nil {
		t.Fatal("TokenUsage nil")
	}
	if r.TokenUsage.Total != 120469 {
		t.Errorf("TokenUsage.Total = %d", r.TokenUsage.Total)
	}
	if r.TokenUsage.Cost != 0.1463847 {
		t.Errorf("TokenUsage.Cost = %v (must be verbatim)", r.TokenUsage.Cost)
	}
	// optionals present here
	if r.DurationMs == nil || *r.DurationMs != 22391 {
		t.Errorf("DurationMs = %v", r.DurationMs)
	}
	if r.CompletedAt == nil {
		t.Error("CompletedAt nil but fixture has it")
	}
	// .result is authoritative RawMessage, must contain "overall"
	var res map[string]json.RawMessage
	if err := json.Unmarshal(r.Result, &res); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Result not an object: %v", err)
	}
	if _, ok := res["overall"]; !ok {
		t.Error("Result missing 'overall'")
	}
	// logs[0] verbatim (used for failure-message sidecar)
	if len(r.Logs) == 0 {
		t.Error("Logs empty")
	}
}

func TestOptionalsAbsentDoNotError(t *testing.T) {
	// A running run omits result/tokenUsage/completedAt/durationMs.
	js := `{"runId":"r1","sessionId":"s1","status":"running","agents":[],"journal":[]}`
	var r Run
	if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(js), &r); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unmarshal partial: %v", err)
	}
	if r.CompletedAt != nil || r.DurationMs != nil || r.TokenUsage != nil {
		t.Error("absent optionals should be nil pointers")
	}
	if len(r.Result) != 0 {
		t.Errorf("absent Result should be empty RawMessage, got %s", r.Result)
	}
}
```

**2b. Run it — expect a COMPILE failure (no model.go yet).**
```
go test ./internal/model/ -run TestUnmarshalSampleRun -v
```
Expected: build error like `undefined: Run`. Good — red phase.

## Task 3 — internal/model: implement to green

**3a. Create `internal/model/model.go`** (COMPLETE):
```go
// Package model defines the wire/domain types for pi-mcp: the pi run-file
// schema (spec §7), the pi --mode json stream events (§7), the MCP tool
// input/output structs (§5), and the persisted job registry record (§8).
//
// Rules (spec §7): optional run-file fields are POINTERS so absence is
// distinguishable from zero; arbitrary workflow output (run .result and
// journal[].result) is json.RawMessage (shape is workflow-defined); Cost is
// float64 read VERBATIM and never recomputed.
package model

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"time"
)

// ---------- pi run file: <launch-cwd>/.pi/workflows/runs/<runId>.json ----------

// Run is the on-disk pi workflow run file. runstore owns the canonical .Result
// when Status=="completed"; the stream parser is only an early/live fallback.
type Run struct {
	RunID        string          `json:"runId"`
	SessionID    string          `json:"sessionId"`
	WorkflowName string          `json:"workflowName"`
	Status       string          `json:"status"` // running|paused|completed|failed|aborted (disk vocabulary)
	CurrentPhase *string         `json:"currentPhase,omitempty"`
	Phases       []string        `json:"phases,omitempty"`
	Agents       []Agent         `json:"agents"`
	Journal      []JournalEntry  `json:"journal"`
	Logs         []string        `json:"logs,omitempty"`
	Script       string          `json:"script,omitempty"`
	Result       json.RawMessage `json:"result,omitempty"`      // workflow-defined shape; authoritative when completed
	StartedAt    *time.Time      `json:"startedAt,omitempty"`
	CompletedAt  *time.Time      `json:"completedAt,omitempty"` // omitted while running/failed
	UpdatedAt    *time.Time      `json:"updatedAt,omitempty"`   // liveness/staleness clock
	DurationMs   *int64          `json:"durationMs,omitempty"`  // only at end
	TokenUsage   *TokenUsage     `json:"tokenUsage,omitempty"`  // only at end
	Args         json.RawMessage `json:"args,omitempty"`        // null in headless; TASK is NOT here
}

// Agent is one entry of run.agents[]. id == callIndex+1. Join to journal by
// CallIndex == JournalEntry.Index (NEVER by array position, NEVER by id).
type Agent struct {
	ID            int        `json:"id"`        // == CallIndex+1
	CallIndex     int        `json:"callIndex"` // join key
	Label         string     `json:"label"`
	Model         string     `json:"model"`
	Phase         string     `json:"phase"`
	Prompt        string     `json:"prompt"`
	Status        string     `json:"status"`        // done|running|error|...
	ResultPreview string     `json:"resultPreview"` // truncated preview only
	Tokens        int64      `json:"tokens"`
	StartedAt     *time.Time `json:"startedAt,omitempty"`
	EndedAt       *time.Time `json:"endedAt,omitempty"`
	Error         *string    `json:"error,omitempty"` // present on agent failure (§9 extraction order #2)
}

// JournalEntry is one entry of run.journal[]. Index == Agent.CallIndex.
// Result is the COMPLETE per-agent output (not a preview). Journal is ordered
// by COMPLETION, not by index (e.g. 0,2,1,3 in the canonical fixture).
type JournalEntry struct {
	Index  int             `json:"index"` // == Agent.CallIndex
	Hash   string          `json:"hash"`
	Result json.RawMessage `json:"result"` // complete per-agent result, workflow-defined shape
}

// TokenUsage is run.tokenUsage (present only at end). Cost is verbatim float64.
type TokenUsage struct {
	Input      int64   `json:"input"`
	Output     int64   `json:"output"`
	Total      int64   `json:"total"`
	Cost       float64 `json:"cost"` // VERBATIM, never recomputed
	CacheRead  int64   `json:"cacheRead"`
	CacheWrite int64   `json:"cacheWrite"`
}

// ---------- pi --mode json stream events (§7) ----------
// Line-delimited JSON; switch on .Type; ignore unknown types.

// StreamEvent is the generic envelope for one JSONL line.
type StreamEvent struct {
	Type    string          `json:"type"`              // session|agent_start|agent_end|turn_start|turn_end|message_start|message_end|tool_execution_start|tool_execution_end|...
	ID      string          `json:"id,omitempty"`      // on type=="session": == run.sessionId
	Version int             `json:"version,omitempty"` // session events
	CWD     string          `json:"cwd,omitempty"`     // session events
	// tool_execution_* fields:
	ToolName   string          `json:"toolName,omitempty"`
	ToolCallID string          `json:"toolCallId,omitempty"`
	IsError    bool            `json:"isError,omitempty"`
	Result     *ToolResult     `json:"result,omitempty"`  // on tool_execution_end
	Args       json.RawMessage `json:"args,omitempty"`    // on tool_execution_start (workflow script etc.)
	Message    json.RawMessage `json:"message,omitempty"` // message_start/message_end payload (unparsed here)
}

// ToolResult is tool_execution_end(toolName=="workflow").result. The workflow
// final result lives in Content[0].Text as: header line + a ```json``` block.
// NOTE (validated §7): it does NOT carry details.result/details.runId — extract
// from Content[0].Text by stripping the "✓ Workflow ... finished" header and
// parsing the fenced json block (fallback: raw text).
type ToolResult struct {
	Content []ContentBlock  `json:"content"`
	Details json.RawMessage `json:"details,omitempty"`
}

// ContentBlock is one block of a ToolResult.Content / message content.
type ContentBlock struct {
	Type string `json:"type"`           // text|thinking|toolCall|...
	Text string `json:"text,omitempty"`
}

// ---------- job registry record, persisted to disk (§8) ----------

// JobStatus is the pi-mcp-level job lifecycle status surfaced to MCP clients.
type JobStatus string

const (
	JobQueued    JobStatus = "queued"
	JobRunning   JobStatus = "running"
	JobCompleted JobStatus = "completed"
	JobFailed    JobStatus = "failed"
	JobAborted   JobStatus = "aborted"
)

// JobMode is the isolation+delivery mode (NOT a capability restriction, §4.1).
type JobMode string

const (
	ModeRead  JobMode = "read"
	ModeWrite JobMode = "write"
)

// JobRecord is persisted (jobId -> record) so write-job runs (inside the
// worktree) can be located and jobs recovered after a restart (§8).
type JobRecord struct {
	JobID        string    `json:"jobId"`        // UUIDv4; registry key + write branch name
	RunID        string    `json:"runId"`        // correlated via sessionId; "" until known
	SessionID    string    `json:"sessionId"`    // from 1st stream "session" event
	Mode         JobMode   `json:"mode"`
	CWD          string    `json:"cwd"`          // resolved absolute launch cwd
	RunsDir      string    `json:"runsDir"`      // <cwd|worktree>/.pi/workflows/runs
	WorktreePath string    `json:"worktreePath,omitempty"` // iff write
	Branch       string    `json:"branch,omitempty"`       // iff write: pi-mcp/job-<jobId>
	PID          int       `json:"pid"`          // os process pid (liveness, same session only)
	Status       JobStatus `json:"status"`
	StartedAt    time.Time `json:"startedAt"`
	ErrorCode    string    `json:"errorCode,omitempty"` // one of config error-code consts
	ErrorMessage string    `json:"errorMessage,omitempty"`
}

// ---------- MCP tool I/O structs (§5) ----------
// Field json names ARE the wire contract. jsonschema tags become the schema
// descriptions consumed by mcp.AddTool reflection.

// --- pi_workflow (§5.1) ---

type WorkflowInput struct {
	Task    string `json:"task" jsonschema:"the task to delegate to the pi dynamic-workflow engine (required)"`
	Mode    string `json:"mode" jsonschema:"isolation+delivery mode: read (in-cwd) or write (git worktree) (required)"`
	CWD     string `json:"cwd" jsonschema:"absolute existing path; rejects '..'; symlinks resolved; never the server cwd (required)"`
	Context string `json:"context,omitempty" jsonschema:"optional extra context appended to the prompt"`
}

type WorkflowOutput struct {
	JobID        string `json:"jobId" jsonschema:"server UUIDv4; registry key and write-branch name"`
	Status       string `json:"status" jsonschema:"queued or running"`
	Mode         string `json:"mode" jsonschema:"read or write"`
	CWD          string `json:"cwd"`
	WorktreePath string `json:"worktree_path,omitempty" jsonschema:"present iff mode=write"`
	StartedAt    string `json:"started_at" jsonschema:"RFC3339 UTC"`
}

// --- pi_status (§5.2) ---

type StatusInput struct {
	JobID string `json:"jobId,omitempty" jsonschema:"job id from pi_workflow"`
	RunID string `json:"runId,omitempty" jsonschema:"alternative: external/post-restart run id (requires cwd)"`
	CWD   string `json:"cwd,omitempty" jsonschema:"required when querying by runId; resolves the runs dir"`
	Wait  bool   `json:"wait,omitempty" jsonschema:"long-poll until a terminal/new-agent/new-phase change (cap 60s)"`
}

// IntermediateResult is one completed agent surfaced live (join index==callIndex).
type IntermediateResult struct {
	Label     string          `json:"label"`
	Model     string          `json:"model"`
	Phase     string          `json:"phase"`
	Result    json.RawMessage `json:"result,omitempty"`         // full journal result; or preview if truncated
	Preview   string          `json:"resultPreview,omitempty"`  // present when Truncated
	Truncated bool            `json:"truncated"`
}

// StatusMetadata mirrors §5.2 metadata; cost/tokens only at end.
type StatusMetadata struct {
	ByModel    map[string]int `json:"by_model"`
	AgentCount int            `json:"agentCount"`
	TokenUsage *TokenUsage    `json:"tokenUsage,omitempty"`
	DurationMs *int64         `json:"durationMs,omitempty"`
}

// WriteInfo is the write-mode delivery block (§4.1/§5.2), present iff write.
type WriteInfo struct {
	Branch       string   `json:"branch"`
	WorktreePath string   `json:"worktree_path"`
	DiffStat     string   `json:"diff_stat"`
	FilesChanged []string `json:"files_changed"`
}

type StatusOutput struct {
	JobID        string               `json:"jobId"`
	RunID        *string              `json:"runId"`               // null during blind window
	Status       string               `json:"status"`              // queued|running|completed|failed|aborted (mapped)
	Phase        *string              `json:"phase"`               // == run.currentPhase; null if unknown
	BlindWindow  bool                 `json:"blind_window"`        // true while run file does not yet exist
	Intermediate []IntermediateResult `json:"intermediate"`        // grows each poll
	Result       json.RawMessage      `json:"result,omitempty"`    // coerced contract (§5.4) when completed
	Metadata     *StatusMetadata      `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Write        *WriteInfo           `json:"write,omitempty"`     // iff write
	Error        string               `json:"error,omitempty"`     // failed/aborted message
}

// --- pi_list (§5.3) ---

type ListInput struct {
	CWD   string `json:"cwd" jsonschema:"required; resolves the runs dir; for write jobs use the worktree_path"`
	Limit int    `json:"limit,omitempty" jsonschema:"max rows (default 20)"`
}

type ListItem struct {
	RunID        string      `json:"runId"`
	WorkflowName string      `json:"workflowName"`
	Status       string      `json:"status"`
	AgentCount   int         `json:"agentCount"`
	ByModel      map[string]int `json:"by_model"`
	Cost         *float64    `json:"cost,omitempty"`       // verbatim; nil until end
	DurationMs   *int64      `json:"durationMs,omitempty"`
	CompletedAt  *time.Time  `json:"completedAt,omitempty"`
}

type ListOutput struct {
	Runs []ListItem `json:"runs"`
}

// --- pi_cancel (§5.5) ---

type CancelInput struct {
	JobID string `json:"jobId" jsonschema:"job id to cancel (required)"`
}

type CancelOutput struct {
	JobID  string `json:"jobId"`
	Status string `json:"status"` // aborted
}
```

## Task 4 — internal/config: failing test first

Pins the constants every package needs: cap, staleness, pi bin, invocation flags, the EXACT forcing-prompt template (§4.2) with placeholders, and the error-code string consts (§9).

**4a. Create `internal/config/config_test.go`:**
```go
package config

import (
	"strings"
	"testing"
	"time"
)

func TestConstants(t *testing.T) {
	if DefaultConcurrencyCap != 4 {
		t.Errorf("cap = %d, want 4", DefaultConcurrencyCap)
	}
	if StaleThreshold != 300*time.Second {
		t.Errorf("StaleThreshold = %v, want 300s", StaleThreshold)
	}
	if DefaultAgentTimeoutMs != 300000 {
		t.Errorf("DefaultAgentTimeoutMs = %d", DefaultAgentTimeoutMs)
	}
	if WaitCap != 60*time.Second {
		t.Errorf("WaitCap = %v, want 60s", WaitCap)
	}
}

func TestPiInvocation(t *testing.T) {
	if PiBinary != "pi" {
		t.Errorf("PiBinary = %q", PiBinary)
	}
	want := []string{"-p", "--mode", "json", "--no-session"}
	if strings.Join(PiBaseFlags, " ") != strings.Join(want, " ") {
		t.Errorf("PiBaseFlags = %v, want %v", PiBaseFlags, want)
	}
	if NoContextFilesFlag != "--no-context-files" {
		t.Errorf("NoContextFilesFlag = %q", NoContextFilesFlag)
	}
}

func TestForcingPromptTemplate(t *testing.T) {
	// Must contain the load-bearing constraints and the placeholders.
	for _, sub := range []string{
		"exactly ONE call",
		"`workflow`",
		"background:false",
		"Do not use background:true",
		"INLINE",
		"{{CONTRACT}}",
		"{{TASK}}",
		"{{CONTEXT}}",
	} {
		if !strings.Contains(ForcingPromptTemplate, sub) {
			t.Errorf("ForcingPromptTemplate missing %q", sub)
		}
	}
	// Contracts must be non-empty and JSON-ish skeletons.
	if !strings.Contains(ReadContractSkeleton, "findings") {
		t.Errorf("ReadContractSkeleton = %q", ReadContractSkeleton)
	}
	if !strings.Contains(WriteContractSkeleton, "files_changed") {
		t.Errorf("WriteContractSkeleton = %q", WriteContractSkeleton)
	}
}

func TestErrorCodes(t *testing.T) {
	if ErrModelRoutingError != "MODEL_ROUTING_ERROR" {
		t.Errorf("ErrModelRoutingError = %q", ErrModelRoutingError)
	}
	if ErrNotAGitRepo != "NOT_A_GIT_REPO" {
		t.Errorf("ErrNotAGitRepo = %q", ErrNotAGitRepo)
	}
	if ErrNoWorkflowRun != "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN" {
		t.Errorf("ErrNoWorkflowRun = %q", ErrNoWorkflowRun)
	}
}
```

```

## Task 5 — internal/config: implement to green

**5a. Create `internal/config/config.go`** (COMPLETE):
```go
// Package config holds pi-mcp's compile-time defaults and string contracts:
// the pi binary + invocation flags (§4), concurrency cap and liveness windows
// (§8), the EXACT forcing-prompt template + output-contract skeletons (§4.2/§5.4),
// and the §9 error-code string constants. Leaf package: no internal deps.
package config

import "time"

// ---- concurrency / liveness (§8) ----
const (
	// DefaultConcurrencyCap is the max simultaneous pi jobs (configurable).
	// Justified by provider rate limits, not a token budget (decision #12).
	DefaultConcurrencyCap = 4

	// DefaultAgentTimeoutMs is the engine's per-agent timeout (~5min). pi-mcp
	// does NOT impose its own job timeout (cancel-only); this mirrors the engine.
	DefaultAgentTimeoutMs int64 = 300000
)

// StaleThreshold: a disk status of "running" with UpdatedAt older than this is
// treated as crashed (post-restart liveness override). 300s == DefaultAgentTimeoutMs.
const StaleThreshold = 300 * time.Second

// WaitCap bounds pi_status long-poll (injectable for tests).
const WaitCap = 60 * time.Second

// ---- pi invocation contract (§4) ----
// Command: pi -p --mode json --no-session [--no-context-files] <PROMPT as single argv>
// stdin MUST be /dev/null; env = os.Environ() passthrough; cwd = project|worktree.
const (
	PiBinary           = "pi"
	NoContextFilesFlag = "--no-context-files"
)

// PiBaseFlags are always passed (the optional NoContextFilesFlag is appended by
// the runner based on config; default ON for code tasks per §4).
var PiBaseFlags = []string{"-p", "--mode", "json", "--no-session"}

// DefaultNoContextFiles: when true, the runner appends NoContextFilesFlag.
// Spec §4: default ON for code tasks (lets pi see AGENTS.md/CLAUDE.md). Note the
// flag literally DISABLES context files, so "default see project files" == do NOT
// pass it. Runner appends the flag only when this is false (hermetic delegation).
const DefaultNoContextFiles = false

// ---- worktree (§4.1) ----
const (
	// WorktreeBranchPrefix + jobID forms the fresh branch: pi-mcp/job-<jobId>.
	WorktreeBranchPrefix = "pi-mcp/job-"
	// WorktreeSubdir under $XDG_STATE_HOME (or temp): pi-mcp/worktrees/.
	WorktreeSubdir = "pi-mcp/worktrees"
)

// ---- runs dir layout (§7) ----
// Run files live at <launch-cwd>/.pi/workflows/runs/<runId>.json
const RunsDirRel = ".pi/workflows/runs"

// ---- result truncation (§5.2) ----
// Intermediate/journal results larger than this are returned as preview+truncated.
const MaxInlineResultBytes = 16 * 1024

// ---- forcing prompt (§4.2) ----
// Source of truth: docs/research/fixtures/sample-forced-workflow-prompt.txt.
// Placeholders: {{CONTRACT}} (read|write skeleton, §5.4), {{TASK}}, {{CONTEXT}}.
// The CONTEXT line/block is included only when context is non-empty (the runner
// trims the "[CONTEXT: ...]" section when {{CONTEXT}} would be empty).
const ForcingPromptTemplate = `You MUST make exactly ONE call to the ` + "`workflow`" + ` tool with background:false. Do not answer
directly. Do not use background:true. Return the final synthesized result INLINE this turn.
Decompose the task as you see fit and fan out subagents in parallel.
The workflow MUST return an object matching exactly this JSON shape:
{{CONTRACT}}

TASK:
{{TASK}}

[CONTEXT:
{{CONTEXT}}]`

// ReadContractSkeleton is the §5.4 read-mode default output shape (requested, not enforced).
const ReadContractSkeleton = `{ "summary": "string", "findings": [ { "title": "string", "detail": "string", "severity": "low|med|high" } ], "confidence": "string", "open_questions": ["string"] }`

// WriteContractSkeleton is the §5.4 write-mode default output shape.
const WriteContractSkeleton = `{ "summary": "string", "files_changed": ["string"], "diff_summary": "string", "tests_run": "string", "notes": "string" }`

// ---- error codes (§9) ----
// Engine WorkflowErrorCode values + pi-mcp-originated codes. String values match
// the engine vocabulary verbatim; surfaced in JobRecord.ErrorCode / StatusOutput.Error.
const (
	ErrModelRoutingError     = "MODEL_ROUTING_ERROR"      // tier/model not authenticated; strict config
	ErrAgentTimeout          = "AGENT_TIMEOUT"            // per-agent engine timeout
	ErrAgentExecutionError   = "AGENT_EXECUTION_ERROR"    // agent run failure
	ErrWorkflowAborted       = "WORKFLOW_ABORTED"         // -> aborted
	ErrAgentLimitExceeded    = "AGENT_LIMIT_EXCEEDED"
	ErrTokenBudgetExhausted  = "TOKEN_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED"
	ErrScriptValidationError = "SCRIPT_VALIDATION_ERROR"
	ErrSchemaNoncompliance   = "SCHEMA_NONCOMPLIANCE"
	ErrPersistenceError      = "PERSISTENCE_ERROR"
	ErrUnknown               = "UNKNOWN"

	// pi-mcp-originated (not engine codes):
	ErrNotAGitRepo   = "NOT_A_GIT_REPO"   // write cwd is not a git repo (fail before spawn)
	ErrNoWorkflowRun = "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN"  // no tool_execution_end(workflow) — trigger not wired (no retry)
)
```

**5b. Run to GREEN.**

## Foundation done — exit criteria
- `go build ./...` and `go vet ./...` clean.
- `go test ./internal/model/ ./internal/config/ -v` all PASS.
- `internal/model` and `internal/config` are LEAF packages (depend only on stdlib + the SDK is referenced only later). Downstream drafters import these for every shared type and constant.
- Hand off to the package drafters using `package_order` (parser/runstore/worktree first, then runner/jobs, then mcpserver, then main_e2e).

### Shared types & signatures (contract for all packages)

CONTRACT every downstream package builds against. Package `pi-mcp/internal/model` (types) and `pi-mcp/internal/config` (consts). All optionals are pointers; all arbitrary workflow output is encoding/json.RawMessage; Cost is float64 verbatim.

=== model (run file, §7) ===
type Run struct{ RunID, SessionID, WorkflowName, Status string; CurrentPhase *string; Phases []string; Agents []Agent; Journal []JournalEntry; Logs []string; Script string; Result json.RawMessage; StartedAt, CompletedAt, UpdatedAt *time.Time; DurationMs *int64; TokenUsage *TokenUsage; Args json.RawMessage }
type Agent struct{ ID int /*==CallIndex+1*/; CallIndex int /*join key*/; Label, Model, Phase, Prompt, Status, ResultPreview string; Tokens int64; StartedAt, EndedAt *time.Time; Error *string }
type JournalEntry struct{ Index int /*==Agent.CallIndex*/; Hash string; Result json.RawMessage /*complete per-agent*/ }
type TokenUsage struct{ Input, Output, Total int64; Cost float64 /*verbatim*/; CacheRead, CacheWrite int64 }
JOIN RULE: journal[i].Index == agents[j].CallIndex (NEVER array position, NEVER agents.ID). Journal ordered by completion (e.g. 0,2,1,3).

=== model (stream events, §7) ===
type StreamEvent struct{ Type string; ID, /*session id*/; Version int; CWD string; ToolName, ToolCallID string; IsError bool; Result *ToolResult; Args json.RawMessage; Message json.RawMessage }
type ToolResult struct{ Content []ContentBlock; Details json.RawMessage }
type ContentBlock struct{ Type, Text string }
PARSER RULE: workflow result = strip "✓ Workflow ... finished" header line from Content[0].Text, parse the ```json``` block (fallback raw). session.ID == Run.SessionID.

=== model (job registry, §8) ===
type JobStatus string; consts JobQueued/JobRunning/JobCompleted/JobFailed/JobAborted ("queued".."aborted")
type JobMode string; consts ModeRead("read"), ModeWrite("write")
type JobRecord struct{ JobID, RunID, SessionID string; Mode JobMode; CWD, RunsDir, WorktreePath, Branch string; PID int; Status JobStatus; StartedAt time.Time; ErrorCode, ErrorMessage string }

=== model (MCP tool I/O, §5) — json+jsonschema tags are the wire contract ===
WorkflowInput{ Task, Mode, CWD, Context string }  -> WorkflowOutput{ JobID, Status, Mode, CWD, WorktreePath, StartedAt string }
StatusInput{ JobID, RunID, CWD string; Wait bool } -> StatusOutput{ JobID string; RunID *string; Status string; Phase *string; BlindWindow bool; Intermediate []IntermediateResult; Result json.RawMessage; Metadata *StatusMetadata; Write *WriteInfo; Error string }
type IntermediateResult struct{ Label, Model, Phase string; Result json.RawMessage; Preview string; Truncated bool }
type StatusMetadata struct{ ByModel map[string]int; AgentCount int; TokenUsage *TokenUsage; DurationMs *int64 }
type WriteInfo struct{ Branch, WorktreePath, DiffStat string; FilesChanged []string }
ListInput{ CWD string; Limit int } -> ListOutput{ Runs []ListItem }
type ListItem struct{ RunID, WorkflowName, Status string; AgentCount int; ByModel map[string]int; Cost *float64; DurationMs *int64; CompletedAt *time.Time }
CancelInput{ JobID string } -> CancelOutput{ JobID, Status string }

=== config consts ===
DefaultConcurrencyCap=4; DefaultAgentTimeoutMs int64=300000; StaleThreshold=300*time.Second; WaitCap=60*time.Second
PiBinary="pi"; PiBaseFlags=[]string{"-p","--mode","json","--no-session"}; NoContextFilesFlag="--no-context-files"; DefaultNoContextFiles=false
WorktreeBranchPrefix="pi-mcp/job-"; WorktreeSubdir="pi-mcp/worktrees"; RunsDirRel=".pi/workflows/runs"; MaxInlineResultBytes=16*1024
ForcingPromptTemplate (placeholders {{CONTRACT}},{{TASK}},{{CONTEXT}}); ReadContractSkeleton; WriteContractSkeleton
Error codes (string consts): ErrModelRoutingError, ErrAgentTimeout, ErrAgentExecutionError, ErrWorkflowAborted, ErrAgentLimitExceeded, ErrTokenBudgetExhausted, ErrScriptValidationError, ErrSchemaNoncompliance, ErrPersistenceError, ErrUnknown, ErrNotAGitRepo, ErrNoWorkflowRun

=== go-sdk usage (mcpserver/main) ===
import "github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"
server := mcp.NewServer(&mcp.Implementation{Name:"pi-mcp",Version:"v0.1.0"}, nil)
mcp.AddTool(server, &mcp.Tool{Name:"pi_workflow",Description:"..."}, handlerWorkflow)  // generic; In/Out structs from model
handler sig: func(ctx context.Context, req *mcp.CallToolRequest, in WorkflowInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, WorkflowOutput, error) { return nil, out, nil }
server.Run(ctx, &mcp.StdioTransport{})

---


## internal/parser — pi -p --mode json stream (JSONL) parser (`parser`)

**Files:** /root/pi-mcp/internal/parser/parser.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/parser/parser_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/parser/result.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/parser/result_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/parser/fixture_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl

_Assumptions:_ The parser does NOT import internal/model: the contract's model.StreamEvent has fields (Version, CWD, ToolCallID, Args, Message) the parser never needs, and the spec (§6) describes parser as owning its own minimal line decode. The plan defines a private streamEvent envelope inside the parser package and returns a small parser.Result struct instead. If the orchestrator requires the parser to reuse model.StreamEvent verbatim, P1/P3 can be retargeted to decode into model.StreamEvent (it has ID, ToolName, IsError, Result *ToolResult, and Result.Content[]ContentBlock — all the fields the parser reads), with no logic change.; config.ErrNoWorkflowRun is a string const equal to "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN" (per the foundation contract). Result.Err() returns this string (the project's error codes are string consts, not Go error values), matching the §9 catalog.; session.id is the top-level `id` field on the session event (verified in the fixture: {"type":"session","id":"019ea2fe-..."}), which equals StreamEvent.ID and Run.SessionID. The parser captures the FIRST session event's id and ignores any later ones.; The fenced block is matched as ```json ... ``` anywhere in content[0].text (verified: exactly one such block, 2 fence markers, header is line 0). The first ```json fence wins; inner bytes are returned verbatim only if json.Valid. All fallbacks (header-strip, whole-text) JSON-string-wrap so Result.Result is ALWAYS valid JSON (never nil except for the no-workflow case where it is left empty).; Malformed individual JSONL lines and unknown .type values are silently ignored (resilient stream parsing); ParseStream returns a non-nil error ONLY on a fatal io read error from the underlying reader.; Scanner buffer set to 1MB max (longest fixture line is 13527 bytes; default bufio 64KB would also suffice, but spec §7 recommends >=1MB headroom since the script can be large — though the script lives in the run file, not a stdout line).; The negative fixture sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl does not yet exist; Task P10 creates it (per §11 Fase 0 'A fazer'). It is a direct-answer stream with a session event but no tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow").; Go is not installed in this build env; all `go build`/`go test`/`go vet` commands are written to be run where Go 1.23+ is installed. Module path is pi-mcp (so import paths are pi-mcp/internal/...).; Repo root for fixture path resolution from internal/parser is two levels up ('..','..'); go test runs with the package dir as cwd, so docs/research/fixtures is reachable relative to the package.

# Package P — `internal/parser` (JSONL stream parser)

Parses the `pi -p --mode json` stdout stream (JSONL). Scans line-by-line, switches on
`.type`, **ignores unknown types**, captures `session.id` (== `Run.SessionID`), detects
`tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow")`, and extracts the workflow result by stripping the
`✓ Workflow ... finished` header line and parsing the fenced ```` ```json ```` block in
`content[0].text` (fallback: raw text). When no workflow `tool_execution_end` is present,
reports `NO_WORKFLOW_RUN`.

**Contract used (from shared foundation, do NOT redefine):**
- `model.StreamEvent`, `model.ToolResult`, `model.ContentBlock` (§7) — live in `internal/model`.
- `config.ErrNoWorkflowRun == "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN"` — lives in `internal/config`.

**Verified fixture facts** (`docs/research/fixtures/sample-pi-mode-json-events.jsonl`, 17 lines):
- Types present: `session, agent_start, turn_start, message_start, message_end, tool_execution_start, tool_execution_end, turn_end, agent_end`.
- `session` line: `{"type":"session","version":3,"id":"019ea2fe-db76-7e31-85ad-9718d3fbc23a","cwd":"/root/pi-mcp",...}` → `id` is **top-level** (maps to `StreamEvent.ID`).
- `tool_execution_end` (workflow): `{"type":"tool_execution_end","toolCallId":"...","toolName":"workflow","result":{"content":[{"type":"text","text":"..."}],"details":{...}},"isError":false}`.
- `content[0].text` line 0 = `✓ Workflow "judge_claims" finished (4 agents · 120,469 tokens · $0.1464 · 22.4s).`; then ```` ```json ````, the object `{claims,overall}`, then ```` ``` ````. Exactly 2 fence markers. Full text len 1027.
- Longest JSONL line = 13527 bytes → scanner buffer must exceed `bufio.MaxScanTokenSize` (64KB is enough, but spec asks ≥1MB to be safe).

> **ENV NOTE:** `go` is NOT installed in this build env. Every "run" step gives the exact
> command + expected output to run where Go (1.23+) IS installed. Do not skip the run steps.

---

## Task P1 — Package skeleton + the public API surface (compile-only)

**File:** `internal/parser/parser.go` (new)

Define the package, the result struct the parser returns, and the parse entrypoint
signatures as stubs that compile (return zero values). This lets every later test compile
against a stable surface.

```go
package parser

import (
	"context"
	"io"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// Result is the outcome of parsing a full pi -p --mode json stream.
type Result struct {
	// SessionID is the id from the first `session` event (== Run.SessionID).
	SessionID string
	// WorkflowFound is true iff a tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow") was seen.
	WorkflowFound bool
	// IsError mirrors that event's isError flag.
	IsError bool
	// RawText is content[0].text of the workflow tool_execution_end (empty if none).
	RawText string
	// Result is the extracted workflow result: the fenced ```json``` block parsed from
	// RawText, or the raw text bytes as a JSON string when no/!invalid fenced block.
	Result model.RawMessageOrNil
}

// ParseStream reads JSONL from r, scanning line-by-line. Unknown event types are ignored.
// It never returns an error for malformed individual lines; it returns an error only on a
// fatal read error from r. Use Result.WorkflowFound to detect NO_WORKFLOW_RUN.
func ParseStream(ctx context.Context, r io.Reader) (Result, error) {
	return Result{}, nil
}
```

> `model.RawMessageOrNil` does not exist in the contract. Replace the field type with
> `json.RawMessage` (import `encoding/json`) — the contract uses `json.RawMessage` for all
> arbitrary workflow output. Corrected code:

```go
package parser

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"io"
)

// Result is the outcome of parsing a full pi -p --mode json stream.
type Result struct {
	SessionID     string
	WorkflowFound bool
	IsError       bool
	RawText       string
	Result        json.RawMessage
}

// ParseStream reads JSONL from r, scanning line-by-line. Unknown event types are ignored.
// It returns an error only on a fatal read error from r (not on malformed lines).
func ParseStream(ctx context.Context, r io.Reader) (Result, error) {
	return Result{}, nil
}
```

## Task P3 — Impl: line scan + decode `.type`, capture session id, ignore unknown

**File:** `internal/parser/parser.go` (replace `ParseStream` body)

Each line is decoded into a small typed envelope. We only need a few fields per type, so
decode the envelope once and branch on `Type`. Unknown types fall through (ignored). Use a
`bufio.Scanner` with a 1MB max buffer (longest fixture line ≈13.5KB; 1MB is safe headroom).

```go
package parser

import (
	"bufio"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"io"
)

const maxLineBytes = 1 << 20 // 1MB scanner buffer (longest fixture line ~13.5KB)

// streamEvent is the minimal envelope we decode per JSONL line. Extra fields on the wire
// are ignored by encoding/json. Unknown .type values simply match no case below.
type streamEvent struct {
	Type     string          `json:"type"`
	ID       string          `json:"id"`       // session.id (top-level)
	ToolName string          `json:"toolName"` // tool_execution_* events
	IsError  bool            `json:"isError"`  // tool_execution_end
	Result   *toolResult     `json:"result"`   // tool_execution_end
}

type toolResult struct {
	Content []contentBlock `json:"content"`
}

type contentBlock struct {
	Type string `json:"type"`
	Text string `json:"text"`
}

// ParseStream reads JSONL from r, scanning line-by-line. Unknown event types are ignored.
// It returns an error only on a fatal read error from r (not on malformed lines).
func ParseStream(ctx context.Context, r io.Reader) (Result, error) {
	var res Result
	sc := bufio.NewScanner(r)
	sc.Buffer(make([]byte, 0, 64*1024), maxLineBytes)

	for sc.Scan() {
		if err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {
			return res, err
		}
		raw := sc.Bytes()
		if len(raw) == 0 {
			continue
		}
		var ev streamEvent
		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &ev); err != nil {
			// Malformed line: ignore (resilient stream parsing), do not abort.
			continue
		}
		switch ev.Type {
		case "session":
			if res.SessionID == "" {
				res.SessionID = ev.ID
			}
		case "tool_execution_end":
			if ev.ToolName == "workflow" {
				res.WorkflowFound = true
				res.IsError = ev.IsError
				if ev.Result != nil && len(ev.Result.Content) > 0 {
					res.RawText = ev.Result.Content[0].Text
				}
				res.Result = extractWorkflowResult(res.RawText)
			}
		default:
			// Unknown / uninteresting type: ignore.
		}
	}
	if err := sc.Err(); err != nil {
		return res, err
	}
	return res, nil
}

// extractWorkflowResult is implemented in result.go (Task P7). Declared here so the package
// compiles after this task; replaced by the real impl in P7. For now return nil.
func extractWorkflowResult(text string) json.RawMessage { return nil }
```

> `extractWorkflowResult` is a temporary stub returning nil so P3 compiles before P7. P7
> replaces this function (move it to `result.go` and delete this stub).

**Run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/parser/ -run TestParseStream_CapturesSessionID
```
Expected: `ok  pi-mcp/internal/parser`.

**Commit:** `parser: scan lines, switch on .type, capture session id`

## Task P6 — Impl: `Result.Err()`

**File:** `internal/parser/parser.go` (add method + import)

```go
// add to the import block:
//   "pi-mcp/internal/config"

// Err returns config.ErrNoWorkflowRun ("NO_WORKFLOW_RUN") when the stream contained no
// tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow"); otherwise "" (no parser-level error). Note:
// IsError (a workflow that ran but failed) is surfaced by the caller, not here.
func (r Result) Err() string {
	if !r.WorkflowFound {
		return config.ErrNoWorkflowRun
	}
	return ""
}
```

## Task P7 — Failing test: extract result from header + fenced ```json``` block

**File:** `internal/parser/result_test.go` (new)

Table-driven over the exact header/fence shape from the fixture, plus fallback cases.

```go
package parser

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"testing"
)

func TestExtractWorkflowResult(t *testing.T) {
	const fenced = "✓ Workflow \"judge_claims\" finished (4 agents · 120,469 tokens · $0.1464 · 22.4s).\n" +
		"```json\n{\n  \"overall\": \"ok\",\n  \"claims\": []\n}\n```"
	const noHeaderFenced = "```json\n{\"a\":1}\n```"
	const rawOnly = "just a plain sentence with no json block"
	const headerThenRaw = "✓ Workflow \"x\" finished (1 agents).\nplain text after header, no fence"

	tests := []struct {
		name      string
		in        string
		wantJSON  string // expected RawMessage as compact JSON; "" means "any string-wrapped"
		wantKeys  []string
		isString  bool   // true when result is a JSON string fallback
		wantStrEq string // expected decoded string value when isString
	}{
		{
			name:     "header + fenced json (fixture shape)",
			in:       fenced,
			wantKeys: []string{"overall", "claims"},
		},
		{
			name:     "fenced json without header line",
			in:       noHeaderFenced,
			wantJSON: `{"a":1}`,
		},
		{
			name:      "no fence -> raw text fallback as JSON string",
			in:        rawOnly,
			isString:  true,
			wantStrEq: rawOnly,
		},
		{
			name:      "header but no fence -> body after header as JSON string",
			in:        headerThenRaw,
			isString:  true,
			wantStrEq: "plain text after header, no fence",
		},
		{
			name:      "empty -> empty JSON string",
			in:        "",
			isString:  true,
			wantStrEq: "",
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range tests {
		t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			got := extractWorkflowResult(tc.in)
			if !json.Valid(got) {
				t.Fatalf("extractWorkflowResult produced invalid JSON: %q", string(got))
			}
			if tc.isString {
				var s string
				if err := json.Unmarshal(got, &s); err != nil {
					t.Fatalf("expected JSON string, got %q (%v)", string(got), err)
				}
				if s != tc.wantStrEq {
					t.Fatalf("string fallback = %q, want %q", s, tc.wantStrEq)
				}
				return
			}
			if tc.wantJSON != "" {
				var a, b interface{}
				_ = json.Unmarshal(got, &a)
				_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.wantJSON), &b)
				ga, _ := json.Marshal(a)
				gb, _ := json.Marshal(b)
				if string(ga) != string(gb) {
					t.Fatalf("json = %s, want %s", ga, gb)
				}
			}
			for _, k := range tc.wantKeys {
				var m map[string]json.RawMessage
				if err := json.Unmarshal(got, &m); err != nil {
					t.Fatalf("expected object, got %q", string(got))
				}
				if _, ok := m[k]; !ok {
					t.Fatalf("result missing key %q in %s", k, string(got))
				}
			}
		})
	}
}
```

**Run (expect FAIL — current `extractWorkflowResult` stub returns nil → invalid JSON):**
```
go test ./internal/parser/ -run TestExtractWorkflowResult
```
Expected: FAIL (`produced invalid JSON: ""`).

**Commit:** `parser: failing table test for header-strip + json-block extraction`

## Task P8 — Impl: `extractWorkflowResult` (header strip + fenced block parse + fallbacks)

**File:** `internal/parser/result.go` (new). **Delete** the temporary
`extractWorkflowResult` stub from `parser.go` (added in P3).

Strategy: (1) find a fenced ```` ```json ```` … ```` ``` ```` block anywhere in `text`; if
present and the inner bytes are valid JSON, return them verbatim (trimmed). (2) Otherwise
strip the leading `✓ Workflow … finished` header line (everything up to and including the
first `\n`) and JSON-string-wrap the remaining body. (3) If there's no header newline either,
JSON-string-wrap the whole text. All fallbacks always yield valid JSON.

```go
package parser

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"strings"
)

const jsonFenceOpen = "```json"
const fence = "```"

// extractWorkflowResult turns the workflow tool_execution_end content[0].text into a
// json.RawMessage. Preference order:
//  1. The first fenced ```json ... ``` block, if its inner bytes are valid JSON -> verbatim.
//  2. The text with the leading "✓ Workflow ... finished" header line stripped, wrapped as
//     a JSON string.
//  3. The whole text wrapped as a JSON string.
// The return value is always valid JSON.
func extractWorkflowResult(text string) json.RawMessage {
	if block, ok := fencedJSONBlock(text); ok {
		trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(block)
		if json.Valid([]byte(trimmed)) {
			return json.RawMessage(trimmed)
		}
	}
	body := stripHeaderLine(text)
	b, _ := json.Marshal(body) // string marshal never errors
	return json.RawMessage(b)
}

// fencedJSONBlock returns the inner content of the first ```json ... ``` block.
func fencedJSONBlock(text string) (string, bool) {
	start := strings.Index(text, jsonFenceOpen)
	if start < 0 {
		return "", false
	}
	// Move past "```json" and an optional single newline.
	inner := text[start+len(jsonFenceOpen):]
	inner = strings.TrimPrefix(inner, "\n")
	end := strings.Index(inner, fence)
	if end < 0 {
		return "", false
	}
	return inner[:end], true
}

// stripHeaderLine removes a leading "✓ Workflow ... finished ..." header line (everything up
// to and including the first newline) when present. If the text has no header marker, it is
// returned unchanged. If there is a header but no trailing newline, the whole text is the
// header and an empty body is returned.
func stripHeaderLine(text string) string {
	if !strings.HasPrefix(text, "✓ Workflow") {
		return text
	}
	if nl := strings.IndexByte(text, '\n'); nl >= 0 {
		return text[nl+1:]
	}
	return ""
}
```

Also remove the stub from `parser.go`:

```go
// DELETE these lines from parser.go (added in P3):
// func extractWorkflowResult(text string) json.RawMessage { return nil }
```

**Run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/parser/ -run TestExtractWorkflowResult
```
Expected: `ok`.

**Commit:** `parser: extractWorkflowResult — fenced json block + header-strip fallbacks`

## Task P9 — Failing test: end-to-end against the real positive fixture

**File:** `internal/parser/fixture_test.go` (new)

Parse the actual `sample-pi-mode-json-events.jsonl` and assert session id, workflow found,
non-error, and the extracted `{claims,overall}` object.

```go
package parser

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"
)

// fixturePath resolves a file under docs/research/fixtures from the repo root. The parser
// package lives at internal/parser, so the repo root is two levels up.
func fixturePath(t *testing.T, name string) string {
	t.Helper()
	p := filepath.Join("..", "..", "docs", "research", "fixtures", name)
	if _, err := os.Stat(p); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("fixture %s not found at %s: %v", name, p, err)
	}
	return p
}

func TestParseStream_PositiveFixture(t *testing.T) {
	f, err := os.Open(fixturePath(t, "sample-pi-mode-json-events.jsonl"))
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatal(err)
	}
	defer f.Close()

	got, err := ParseStream(context.Background(), f)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("ParseStream error: %v", err)
	}
	if got.SessionID != "019ea2fe-db76-7e31-85ad-9718d3fbc23a" {
		t.Fatalf("SessionID = %q", got.SessionID)
	}
	if !got.WorkflowFound {
		t.Fatal("WorkflowFound = false, want true")
	}
	if got.IsError {
		t.Fatal("IsError = true, want false")
	}
	if e := got.Err(); e != "" {
		t.Fatalf("Err() = %q, want \"\"", e)
	}
	var obj map[string]json.RawMessage
	if err := json.Unmarshal(got.Result, &obj); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Result not an object: %q (%v)", string(got.Result), err)
	}
	for _, k := range []string{"claims", "overall"} {
		if _, ok := obj[k]; !ok {
			t.Fatalf("Result missing key %q: %s", k, string(got.Result))
		}
	}
}
```

**Run (expect PASS — all impl already in place from P3/P8):**
```
go test ./internal/parser/ -run TestParseStream_PositiveFixture
```
Expected: `ok`. (If FAIL, inspect `got.Result` — most likely the fence parse; do not edit
the fixture.)

**Commit:** `parser: e2e test against real sample-pi-mode-json-events.jsonl`
