## Task M5 — Output-contract coercion (§5.4) (test FIRST)

**Step 1 — write failing test** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/coerce_test.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"testing"
)

func TestCoerceResult(t *testing.T) {
	// (a) object already in read shape -> passthrough (summary preserved)
	a := json.RawMessage(`{"summary":"ok","findings":[],"confidence":"high","open_questions":[]}`)
	gotA, warnA := coerceResult(a, "completed")
	if warnA {
		t.Fatalf("(a) should not warn")
	}
	var ma map[string]any
	_ = json.Unmarshal(gotA, &ma)
	if ma["summary"] != "ok" {
		t.Fatalf("(a) summary lost: %s", gotA)
	}

	// (b) bare string scalar -> {summary:<raw>}
	b := json.RawMessage(`"just a string"`)
	gotB, _ := coerceResult(b, "completed")
	var mb map[string]any
	if err := json.Unmarshal(gotB, &mb); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("(b) not an object: %s", gotB)
	}
	if mb["summary"] != "just a string" {
		t.Fatalf("(b) want summary=raw, got %s", gotB)
	}

	// (c) object with different keys (fixture {claims,overall}) -> summary added, originals preserved
	c := json.RawMessage(`{"claims":[1,2,3],"overall":"two true one false"}`)
	gotC, _ := coerceResult(c, "completed")
	var mc map[string]any
	_ = json.Unmarshal(gotC, &mc)
	if _, ok := mc["claims"]; !ok {
		t.Fatalf("(c) original key 'claims' dropped: %s", gotC)
	}
	if _, ok := mc["overall"]; !ok {
		t.Fatalf("(c) original key 'overall' dropped: %s", gotC)
	}
	if _, ok := mc["summary"]; !ok {
		t.Fatalf("(c) summary not synthesized: %s", gotC)
	}
	// 'overall' is used as the summary text when present.
	if mc["summary"] != "two true one false" {
		t.Fatalf("(c) summary should reuse overall: %s", gotC)
	}

	// (d) absent result in completed -> {summary:""} + warn
	gotD, warnD := coerceResult(nil, "completed")
	if !warnD {
		t.Fatalf("(d) expected warn")
	}
	var md map[string]any
	_ = json.Unmarshal(gotD, &md)
	if md["summary"] != "" {
		t.Fatalf("(d) want empty summary, got %s", gotD)
	}

	// non-completed + nil -> nil passthrough (no synthesis mid-run)
	if got, _ := coerceResult(nil, "running"); got != nil {
		t.Fatalf("running+nil should stay nil, got %s", got)
	}
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect FAIL):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestCoerceResult -v   # expect: FAIL (undefined coerceResult)
```

**Step 3 — impl** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/coerce.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"encoding/json"
)

// coerceResult applies the §5.4 best-effort output-contract coercion.
// Returns the coerced JSON and a warn flag (true when a result was expected but missing).
// It NEVER discards original data.
func coerceResult(raw json.RawMessage, mcpStatus string) (json.RawMessage, bool) {
	if len(raw) == 0 {
		if mcpStatus == "completed" {
			// (d) absent in completed -> {summary:""} + warn
			return json.RawMessage(`{"summary":""}`), true
		}
		// mid-run: nothing to coerce yet
		return nil, false
	}

	// Try as object first.
	var obj map[string]json.RawMessage
	if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &obj); err == nil {
		if _, hasSummary := obj["summary"]; hasSummary {
			// (a) already in shape -> passthrough
			return raw, false
		}
		// (c) different keys -> add summary, preserve originals.
		summary := synthSummary(obj)
		obj["summary"] = mustJSON(summary)
		return mustJSON(obj), false
	}

	// Try as a JSON string scalar.
	var s string
	if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &s); err == nil {
		return mustJSON(map[string]string{"summary": s}), false
	}

	// Any other scalar (number/bool/array): stringify into summary, preserve raw alongside.
	return mustJSON(map[string]json.RawMessage{
		"summary": mustJSON(string(raw)),
		"value":   raw,
	}), false
}

// synthSummary picks a human summary string from common keys, else a compact synopsis.
func synthSummary(obj map[string]json.RawMessage) string {
	for _, k := range []string{"overall", "summary_text", "conclusion", "result"} {
		if v, ok := obj[k]; ok {
			var s string
			if json.Unmarshal(v, &s) == nil && s != "" {
				return s
			}
		}
	}
	// fallback: list the keys present so nothing is silently lost.
	keys := make([]string, 0, len(obj))
	for k := range obj {
		keys = append(keys, k)
	}
	b, _ := json.Marshal(keys)
	return "result with keys " + string(b)
}

func mustJSON(v any) json.RawMessage {
	b, err := json.Marshal(v)
	if err != nil {
		return json.RawMessage(`null`)
	}
	return b
}
```

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestCoerceResult -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/coerce*.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: §5.4 output-contract coercion"`

## Task M6 — Intermediate builder (journal↔agents join) + metadata histogram (test FIRST)

**Step 1 — write failing test** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/intermediate_test.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// buildRun mirrors the out-of-order sample-run.json shape (journal completion order 0,2,1,3).
func buildRun() *model.Run {
	return &model.Run{
		RunID:        "mq40rdpt-yij9hj",
		SessionID:    "019ea2fe-db76-7e31-85ad-9718d3fbc23a",
		WorkflowName: "judge_claims",
		Status:       "completed",
		CurrentPhase: strptr("Final"),
		Phases:       []string{"Scan", "Final"},
		Agents: []model.Agent{
			{ID: 1, CallIndex: 0, Label: "claim A", Model: "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash", Phase: "Scan", Status: "done", ResultPreview: "{\"claim\":\"A...", Tokens: 31514},
			{ID: 2, CallIndex: 1, Label: "claim B", Model: "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash", Phase: "Scan", Status: "done", ResultPreview: "{\"claim\":\"B...", Tokens: 31561},
			{ID: 3, CallIndex: 2, Label: "claim C", Model: "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash", Phase: "Scan", Status: "done", ResultPreview: "{\"claim\":\"C...", Tokens: 31568},
			{ID: 4, CallIndex: 3, Label: "final synthesis", Model: "openai-codex/gpt-5.5", Phase: "Final", Status: "done", ResultPreview: "{\"claims\":...", Tokens: 25826},
		},
		Journal: []model.JournalEntry{
			{Index: 0, Result: json.RawMessage(`{"claim":"A","verdict":"TRUE"}`)},
			{Index: 2, Result: json.RawMessage(`{"claim":"C","verdict":"TRUE"}`)},
			{Index: 1, Result: json.RawMessage(`{"claim":"B","verdict":"FALSE"}`)},
			{Index: 3, Result: json.RawMessage(`{"claims":[],"overall":"done"}`)},
		},
		TokenUsage: &model.TokenUsage{Input: 116075, Output: 938, Total: 120469, Cost: 0.1463847},
		DurationMs: i64ptr(22391),
	}
}

func TestBuildIntermediate_JoinByIndex(t *testing.T) {
	got := buildIntermediate(buildRun(), 1024)
	if len(got) != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("want 4 intermediate, got %d", len(got))
	}
	// journal index 2 must join agent callIndex 2 == "claim C", NOT array position 1.
	second := got[1] // journal completion order -> second completed is index 2
	if second.Label != "claim C" {
		t.Fatalf("join wrong: want 'claim C' got %q", second.Label)
	}
	if second.Model != "deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash" || second.Phase != "Scan" {
		t.Fatalf("join wrong model/phase: %+v", second)
	}
	var r map[string]any
	if err := json.Unmarshal(second.Result, &r); err != nil || r["claim"] != "C" {
		t.Fatalf("result wrong for index 2: %s", second.Result)
	}
	if second.Truncated {
		t.Fatalf("short result should not be truncated")
	}
}

func TestBuildIntermediate_Truncation(t *testing.T) {
	run := buildRun()
	big := `{"x":"` + strings.Repeat("z", 200) + `"}`
	run.Journal = []model.JournalEntry{{Index: 0, Result: json.RawMessage(big)}}
	run.Agents = run.Agents[:1]
	got := buildIntermediate(run, 16) // tiny limit forces truncation
	if len(got) != 1 {
		t.Fatalf("want 1, got %d", len(got))
	}
	if !got[0].Truncated {
		t.Fatalf("expected Truncated=true")
	}
	if got[0].Preview == "" {
		t.Fatalf("expected non-empty Preview when truncated")
	}
	if len(got[0].Result) != 0 {
		t.Fatalf("truncated entry should omit full Result, got %s", got[0].Result)
	}
}

func TestBuildIntermediate_OrphanJournalSkipped(t *testing.T) {
	run := buildRun()
	// journal index 9 has no matching agent; must be skipped, not panic.
	run.Journal = append(run.Journal, model.JournalEntry{Index: 9, Result: json.RawMessage(`{}`)})
	got := buildIntermediate(run, 1024)
	if len(got) != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("orphan journal entry must be skipped, got %d", len(got))
	}
}

func TestBuildMetadata(t *testing.T) {
	md := buildMetadata(buildRun())
	if md.AgentCount != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("agentCount want 4 got %d", md.AgentCount)
	}
	if md.ByModel["deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash"] != 3 || md.ByModel["openai-codex/gpt-5.5"] != 1 {
		t.Fatalf("by_model histogram wrong: %v", md.ByModel)
	}
	if md.TokenUsage == nil || md.TokenUsage.Cost != 0.1463847 {
		t.Fatalf("cost must be verbatim, got %+v", md.TokenUsage)
	}
	if md.DurationMs == nil || *md.DurationMs != 22391 {
		t.Fatalf("durationMs wrong: %+v", md.DurationMs)
	}
}

func TestBuildMetadata_SuppressCostMidRun(t *testing.T) {
	run := buildRun()
	run.TokenUsage = nil // mid-run: cost/tokens absent
	run.DurationMs = nil
	md := buildMetadata(run)
	if md.TokenUsage != nil {
		t.Fatalf("tokenUsage must stay nil mid-run")
	}
	if md.AgentCount != 4 {
		t.Fatalf("agentCount should still count agents: %d", md.AgentCount)
	}
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect FAIL):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run 'TestBuildIntermediate|TestBuildMetadata' -v   # expect: FAIL
```

**Step 3 — impl** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/intermediate.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"encoding/json"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// buildIntermediate joins journal[].Index == agents[].CallIndex (NEVER array position,
// NEVER agents[].ID). Journal order (completion order) is preserved. Entries whose Result
// exceeds maxBytes are returned truncated (Preview + Truncated=true, full Result omitted).
func buildIntermediate(run *model.Run, maxBytes int) []model.IntermediateResult {
	byCall := make(map[int]model.Agent, len(run.Agents))
	for _, a := range run.Agents {
		byCall[a.CallIndex] = a
	}
	out := make([]model.IntermediateResult, 0, len(run.Journal))
	for _, j := range run.Journal {
		a, ok := byCall[j.Index] // join key
		if !ok {
			continue // orphan journal entry (no matching agent) -> skip
		}
		ir := model.IntermediateResult{
			Label: a.Label,
			Model: a.Model,
			Phase: a.Phase,
		}
		if len(j.Result) > maxBytes {
			ir.Truncated = true
			ir.Preview = preview(j.Result, maxBytes)
			// Result omitted when truncated.
		} else {
			ir.Result = j.Result
		}
		out = append(out, ir)
	}
	return out
}

func preview(raw json.RawMessage, maxBytes int) string {
	s := string(raw)
	if len(s) <= maxBytes {
		return s
	}
	if maxBytes <= 0 {
		return ""
	}
	return s[:maxBytes]
}

// buildMetadata computes the model histogram + agentCount and passes tokenUsage/durationMs
// through VERBATIM (nil mid-run so cost is suppressed until the run finishes).
func buildMetadata(run *model.Run) *model.StatusMetadata {
	byModel := make(map[string]int)
	for _, a := range run.Agents {
		if a.Model != "" {
			byModel[a.Model]++
		}
	}
	return &model.StatusMetadata{
		ByModel:    byModel,
		AgentCount: len(run.Agents),
		TokenUsage: run.TokenUsage, // verbatim; nil mid-run
		DurationMs: run.DurationMs, // nil mid-run
	}
}
```

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run 'TestBuildIntermediate|TestBuildMetadata' -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/intermediate*.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: journal<->agents join + metadata histogram"`

## Task M7 — `pi_workflow` handler (test FIRST)

**Step 1 — write failing test** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_workflow_test.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"context"
	"testing"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func newServerWith(j JobsService, s RunStore) *Server {
	return New(j, s) // wait poll interval defaulted; clock = time.Now
}

func TestWorkflow_ValidationErrors(t *testing.T) {
	srv := newServerWith(newFakeJobs(), newFakeStore())
	dir := t.TempDir()

	cases := []model.WorkflowInput{
		{Task: "t", Mode: "", CWD: dir},        // missing mode
		{Task: "t", Mode: "read", CWD: ""},     // missing cwd
		{Task: "t", Mode: "read", CWD: "rel"},  // relative cwd
		{Task: "", Mode: "read", CWD: dir},     // missing task
		{Task: "t", Mode: "bogus", CWD: dir},   // bad mode
	}
	for i, in := range cases {
		_, _, err := srv.handleWorkflow(context.Background(), nil, in)
		if err == nil {
			t.Fatalf("case %d expected validation error, got nil", i)
		}
	}
}

func TestWorkflow_SubmitReadHappy(t *testing.T) {
	j := newFakeJobs()
	j.submitRec = model.JobRecord{
		JobID:     "job-123",
		Mode:      model.ModeRead,
		Status:    model.JobRunning,
		CWD:       "/resolved/cwd",
		StartedAt: mustTime("2026-06-07T16:51:33Z"),
	}
	srv := newServerWith(j, newFakeStore())
	dir := t.TempDir()

	_, out, err := srv.handleWorkflow(context.Background(), nil, model.WorkflowInput{
		Task: "judge claims", Mode: "read", CWD: dir, Context: "ctx",
	})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unexpected error: %v", err)
	}
	if out.JobID != "job-123" || out.Status != "running" || out.Mode != "read" {
		t.Fatalf("bad output: %+v", out)
	}
	if out.WorktreePath != "" {
		t.Fatalf("read mode must not return worktree_path: %q", out.WorktreePath)
	}
	if out.StartedAt == "" {
		t.Fatalf("started_at must be set (RFC3339)")
	}
	// spec must carry the RESOLVED cwd (symlink-resolved temp dir), not the raw input.
	if j.lastSpec.CWD == "" || j.lastSpec.Task != "judge claims" || j.lastSpec.Mode != model.ModeRead {
		t.Fatalf("spec not built correctly: %+v", j.lastSpec)
	}
}

func TestWorkflow_SubmitWriteReturnsWorktree(t *testing.T) {
	j := newFakeJobs()
	j.submitRec = model.JobRecord{
		JobID: "job-w", Mode: model.ModeWrite, Status: model.JobQueued,
		CWD: "/c", WorktreePath: "/state/pi-mcp/worktrees/job-w",
		StartedAt: mustTime("2026-06-07T16:51:33Z"),
	}
	srv := newServerWith(j, newFakeStore())
	dir := t.TempDir()
	_, out, err := srv.handleWorkflow(context.Background(), nil, model.WorkflowInput{
		Task: "fix bug", Mode: "write", CWD: dir,
	})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unexpected error: %v", err)
	}
	if out.Status != "queued" || out.Mode != "write" {
		t.Fatalf("bad output: %+v", out)
	}
	if out.WorktreePath != "/state/pi-mcp/worktrees/job-w" {
		t.Fatalf("write must surface worktree_path, got %q", out.WorktreePath)
	}
}
```

**Step 4 — impl Server struct** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/server.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"time"
)

// Server holds the dependencies the handlers need and tunables for long-poll.
type Server struct {
	jobs  JobsService
	store RunStore

	now          func() time.Time // injectable clock (tests)
	waitCap      time.Duration    // long-poll cap
	pollInterval time.Duration    // long-poll tick

	// pidAlive reports whether the job's process is alive (same session). Injected so
	// tests can simulate dead processes; defaults to "assume alive" when nil.
	pidAlive func(pid int) bool
}

// New builds a Server with production defaults.
func New(jobs JobsService, store RunStore) *Server {
	return &Server{
		jobs:         jobs,
		store:        store,
		now:          time.Now,
		waitCap:      defaultWaitCap,
		pollInterval: defaultPollInterval,
		pidAlive:     func(int) bool { return true },
	}
}
```

**Step 5 — impl `pi_workflow`** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_workflow.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"strings"
	"time"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func (s *Server) handleWorkflow(ctx context.Context, _ *mcp.CallToolRequest, in model.WorkflowInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, model.WorkflowOutput, error) {
	var zero model.WorkflowOutput
	if strings.TrimSpace(in.Task) == "" {
		return nil, zero, fmt.Errorf("task is required")
	}
	mode, err := validateMode(in.Mode)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, zero, err
	}
	cwd, err := validateCWD(in.CWD)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, zero, err
	}

	rec, err := s.jobs.Submit(ctx, JobSpec{
		Task:    in.Task,
		Mode:    mode,
		CWD:     cwd,
		Context: in.Context,
	})
	if err != nil {
		return nil, zero, err
	}

	out := model.WorkflowOutput{
		JobID:     rec.JobID,
		Status:    string(rec.Status),
		Mode:      string(rec.Mode),
		CWD:       rec.CWD,
		StartedAt: rec.StartedAt.UTC().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}
	if rec.Mode == model.ModeWrite {
		out.WorktreePath = rec.WorktreePath
	}
	return nil, out, nil
}
```

**Step 6 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestWorkflow -v   # expect: PASS
```

## Task M8 — long-poll constants + wake-predicate snapshot (test FIRST)

**Step 1 — write failing test** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_status_test.go` (predicate part):
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"testing"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func TestWakeChanged(t *testing.T) {
	base := snapshot{journalLen: 2, agentsLen: 3, phase: "Scan", terminal: false}

	// identical -> no wake
	if wakeChanged(base, base) {
		t.Fatalf("identical snapshots should not wake")
	}
	// journal grew -> wake
	g := base
	g.journalLen = 3
	if !wakeChanged(base, g) {
		t.Fatalf("journal growth should wake")
	}
	// agents grew -> wake
	g = base
	g.agentsLen = 4
	if !wakeChanged(base, g) {
		t.Fatalf("agents growth should wake")
	}
	// phase changed -> wake
	g = base
	g.phase = "Final"
	if !wakeChanged(base, g) {
		t.Fatalf("phase change should wake")
	}
	// terminal -> wake
	g = base
	g.terminal = true
	if !wakeChanged(base, g) {
		t.Fatalf("terminal should wake")
	}
}

func TestSnapshotOf_IgnoresRunningPausedFlap(t *testing.T) {
	r := buildRun()
	r.Status = "running"
	a := snapshotOf(r)
	r.Status = "paused" // flap; both map to "running" -> not terminal, same phase/lens
	b := snapshotOf(r)
	if wakeChanged(a, b) {
		t.Fatalf("running<->paused flap must NOT wake")
	}
}

func TestSnapshotOf_NilPhase(t *testing.T) {
	r := &model.Run{Status: "running"} // CurrentPhase nil
	s := snapshotOf(r)
	if s.phase != "" {
		t.Fatalf("nil currentPhase -> empty phase, got %q", s.phase)
	}
	if s.terminal {
		t.Fatalf("running is not terminal")
	}
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect FAIL):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run 'TestWakeChanged|TestSnapshotOf' -v   # expect: FAIL
```

**Step 3 — impl: add constants + snapshot to** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_status.go` (constants block + predicate; the full handler is added in M9 — this step adds only the pieces under test):
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"time"

	"pi-mcp/internal/config"
	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

const (
	defaultWaitCap      = config.WaitCap
	defaultPollInterval = 250 * time.Millisecond
)

// snapshot captures the long-poll wake inputs. running<->paused is collapsed via mapDiskStatus
// (both -> "running") so flapping never triggers a wake.
type snapshot struct {
	journalLen int
	agentsLen  int
	phase      string
	terminal   bool
}

func snapshotOf(run *model.Run) snapshot {
	phase := ""
	if run.CurrentPhase != nil {
		phase = *run.CurrentPhase
	}
	return snapshot{
		journalLen: len(run.Journal),
		agentsLen:  len(run.Agents),
		phase:      phase,
		terminal:   isTerminal(mapDiskStatus(run.Status)),
	}
}

// wakeChanged reports whether the long-poll should return: terminal reached, OR journal grew,
// OR agents grew, OR phase changed. (running<->paused is excluded by construction.)
func wakeChanged(prev, cur snapshot) bool {
	if cur.terminal {
		return true
	}
	if cur.journalLen > prev.journalLen {
		return true
	}
	if cur.agentsLen > prev.agentsLen {
		return true
	}
	if cur.phase != prev.phase {
		return true
	}
	return false
}
```

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run 'TestWakeChanged|TestSnapshotOf' -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/handler_status.go internal/mcpserver/handler_status_test.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: long-poll wake predicate + snapshot"`

```go
func TestStatus_BlindWindow(t *testing.T) {
```

**Step 3 — impl: append the handler to** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_status.go`:
```go
import (
	"context"
	"errors"
	"time"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/config"
	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// resolved identifies where the run file lives and whether an owning job exists.
type resolved struct {
	runsDir  string
	runID    string
	jobID    string
	mode     model.JobMode
	pid      int
	hasJob   bool
	worktree string
	branch   string
}

// resolveTarget turns StatusInput into a runsDir+runID via the jobId path or the runId+cwd path.
func (s *Server) resolveTarget(in model.StatusInput) (resolved, error) {
	if in.JobID != "" {
		rec, ok := s.jobs.Lookup(in.JobID)
		if !ok {
			return resolved{}, errors.New("unknown jobId: " + in.JobID)
		}
		return resolved{
			runsDir: rec.RunsDir, runID: rec.RunID, jobID: rec.JobID, mode: rec.Mode,
			pid: rec.PID, hasJob: true, worktree: rec.WorktreePath, branch: rec.Branch,
		}, nil
	}
	if in.RunID == "" || in.CWD == "" {
		return resolved{}, errors.New("provide jobId, or runId+cwd")
	}
	cwd, err := validateCWD(in.CWD)
	if err != nil {
		return resolved{}, err
	}
	r := resolved{runsDir: runsDirFor(cwd), runID: in.RunID}
	if rec, ok := s.jobs.LookupByRun(in.RunID, cwd); ok {
		r.jobID, r.mode, r.pid, r.hasJob = rec.JobID, rec.Mode, rec.PID, true
		r.worktree, r.branch = rec.WorktreePath, rec.Branch
		if rec.RunsDir != "" {
			r.runsDir = rec.RunsDir
		}
	}
	return r, nil
}

func runsDirFor(cwd string) string {
	return cwd + "/" + config.RunsDirRel
}

func (s *Server) handleStatus(ctx context.Context, _ *mcp.CallToolRequest, in model.StatusInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, model.StatusOutput, error) {
	tgt, err := s.resolveTarget(in)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, model.StatusOutput{}, err
	}

	if in.Wait {
		s.waitForChange(ctx, tgt)
	}

	out := s.buildStatus(tgt)
	return nil, out, nil
}

// buildStatus loads the run file once and assembles StatusOutput (no waiting).
func (s *Server) buildStatus(tgt resolved) model.StatusOutput {
	out := model.StatusOutput{JobID: tgt.jobID}

	run, err := s.store.Load(tgt.runsDir, tgt.runID)
	if err != nil {
		if errors.Is(err, ErrRunNotFound) {
			if tgt.hasJob {
				// owning job exists but run file absent -> blind window
				out.Status = "running"
				out.BlindWindow = true
				return out
			}
			// runId path for a run that does not exist yet -> queued/pending, NOT an error
			out.Status = "queued"
			return out
		}
		// genuine read/parse error
		out.Status = "failed"
		out.Error = config.ErrPersistenceError
		return out
	}

	rid := run.RunID
	out.RunID = &rid
	if run.CurrentPhase != nil {
		ph := *run.CurrentPhase
		out.Phase = &ph
	}

	out.Status = liveStatus(run.Status, run.UpdatedAt, s.now(), s.pidIsAlive(tgt))
	out.Intermediate = buildIntermediate(run, config.MaxInlineResultBytes)
	out.Metadata = buildMetadata(run)

	if out.Status == "completed" {
		res, _ := coerceResult(run.Result, out.Status)
		out.Result = res
	}
	if out.Status == "failed" || out.Status == "aborted" {
		out.Error = failureMessage(run)
	}

	if tgt.mode == model.ModeWrite && tgt.hasJob {
		out.Write = &model.WriteInfo{
			Branch:       tgt.branch,
			WorktreePath: tgt.worktree,
			// DiffStat / FilesChanged are filled by the worktree layer via jobs; left empty
			// here when not yet available (Fase 1 surfaces them through the JobRecord later).
		}
	}
	return out
}

func (s *Server) pidIsAlive(tgt resolved) bool {
	if !tgt.hasJob || tgt.pid == 0 || s.pidAlive == nil {
		return true // no liveness signal -> assume alive (do not falsely fail external runs)
	}
	return s.pidAlive(tgt.pid)
}

// failureMessage follows §9 extraction order: agents[].error, else logs[0] verbatim, else generic.
func failureMessage(run *model.Run) string {
	for _, a := range run.Agents {
		if a.Status == "error" && a.Error != nil && *a.Error != "" {
			return *a.Error
		}
	}
	if len(run.Logs) > 0 {
		return run.Logs[0] // verbatim; never reconstruct the mangled prefix
	}
	return config.ErrUnknown
}

// waitForChange long-polls until the wake predicate fires or the wait cap elapses.
func (s *Server) waitForChange(ctx context.Context, tgt resolved) {
	deadline := s.now().Add(s.waitCap)
	var base snapshot
	haveBase := false

	ticker := time.NewTicker(s.pollInterval)
	defer ticker.Stop()

	for {
		run, err := s.store.Load(tgt.runsDir, tgt.runID)
		if err == nil {
			cur := snapshotOf(run)
			if !haveBase {
				base, haveBase = cur, true
				if cur.terminal {
					return
				}
			} else if wakeChanged(base, cur) {
				return
			}
		}
		if !s.now().Before(deadline) {
			return
		}
		select {
		case <-ctx.Done():
			return
		case <-ticker.C:
		}
	}
}
```
> Implementation note: this step adds new imports to `handler_status.go`. Merge them with the
> import block created in M8 (`time`, `config`, `model`) — final imports: `context`, `errors`,
> `time`, the go-sdk `mcp`, `pi-mcp/internal/config`, `pi-mcp/internal/model`.

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestStatus -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/handler_status*.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: pi_status handler (blind window, mapping, intermediate, coercion, write)"`

## Task M10 — `pi_status` long-poll wake-on-new-agent (integration test FIRST)

**Step 1 — extend** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_status_test.go`:
```go
func TestStatus_WaitWakesOnJournalGrowth(t *testing.T) {
	// Load #1: running, journal len 1. Load #2+: journal len 2 -> wake.
	r1 := buildRun()
	r1.Status = "running"
	r1.Journal = r1.Journal[:1] // index 0 only
	r1.Result = nil
	r1.TokenUsage = nil

	r2 := buildRun()
	r2.Status = "running"
	r2.Journal = r2.Journal[:2] // index 0,2 -> grew
	r2.Result = nil
	r2.TokenUsage = nil

	store := newFakeStore()
	store.seq = []*model.Run{r1, r2} // successive Loads
	j := newFakeJobs()
	j.lookup["job-lp"] = model.JobRecord{JobID: "job-lp", RunsDir: "/runs", RunID: r1.RunID, PID: 1, Status: model.JobRunning}
	srv := New(j, store)
	srv.pollInterval = time.Millisecond
	srv.waitCap = 2 * time.Second

	_, out, err := srv.handleStatus(ctxBG(), nil, model.StatusInput{JobID: "job-lp", Wait: true})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unexpected: %v", err)
	}
	if out.Status != "running" {
		t.Fatalf("want running, got %q", out.Status)
	}
	// after wake, buildStatus loads again (seq sticks to last) -> 2 intermediate
	if len(out.Intermediate) != 2 {
		t.Fatalf("want 2 intermediate after wake, got %d", len(out.Intermediate))
	}
}

func TestStatus_WaitCapReturnsWithoutChange(t *testing.T) {
	r := buildRun()
	r.Status = "running"
	r.Result = nil
	r.TokenUsage = nil
	store := newFakeStore()
	store.runs["/runs/"+r.RunID] = r // same value every Load -> never wakes
	j := newFakeJobs()
	j.lookup["job-cap"] = model.JobRecord{JobID: "job-cap", RunsDir: "/runs", RunID: r.RunID, PID: 1, Status: model.JobRunning}
	srv := New(j, store)
	srv.pollInterval = time.Millisecond
	srv.waitCap = 20 * time.Millisecond // tiny cap -> returns quickly

	done := make(chan struct{})
	go func() {
		_, _, _ = srv.handleStatus(ctxBG(), nil, model.StatusInput{JobID: "job-cap", Wait: true})
		close(done)
	}()
	select {
	case <-done:
	case <-time.After(2 * time.Second):
		t.Fatalf("wait did not return at cap")
	}
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect PASS — logic already implemented in M9; this validates wait wiring):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run 'TestStatus_Wait' -v   # expect: PASS
```
> If FAIL: the fakeStore.seq stepping (M2) or waitForChange deadline check (M9) needs the fix
> indicated by the failure; correct, re-run until PASS.

**Step 3 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/handler_status_test.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: long-poll wake-on-new-agent + cap tests"`

## Task M11 — `pi_list` handler (test FIRST)

**Step 1 — write failing test** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_list_test.go`:

```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"testing"
	"time"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func TestList_HappyAndDefaultLimit(t *testing.T) {

	cost := 0.1463847

func TestList_CWDValidated(t *testing.T) {
	srv := New(newFakeJobs(), newFakeStore())
	if _, _, err := srv.handleList(ctxBG(), nil, model.ListInput{CWD: ""}); err == nil {
		t.Fatalf("empty cwd must error")
	}
	if _, _, err := srv.handleList(ctxBG(), nil, model.ListInput{CWD: "rel/path"}); err == nil {
		t.Fatalf("relative cwd must error")
	}
}

func TestList_StorePassesResolvedLimit(t *testing.T) {
	store := &capturingStore{fakeStore: newFakeStore()}
	srv := New(newFakeJobs(), store)
	dir := t.TempDir()
	_, _, _ = srv.handleList(ctxBG(), nil, model.ListInput{CWD: dir, Limit: 0})
	if store.gotLimit != defaultListLimit {
		t.Fatalf("limit<=0 should default to %d, got %d", defaultListLimit, store.gotLimit)
	}
	_, _, _ = srv.handleList(ctxBG(), nil, model.ListInput{CWD: dir, Limit: 5})
	if store.gotLimit != 5 {
		t.Fatalf("explicit limit not passed, got %d", store.gotLimit)
	}
	_ = time.Now
}

type capturingStore struct {
	*fakeStore
	gotCWD   string
	gotLimit int
}

func (c *capturingStore) ListItems(cwd string, limit int) ([]model.ListItem, error) {
	c.gotCWD, c.gotLimit = cwd, limit
	return c.fakeStore.ListItems(cwd, limit)
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect FAIL):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestList -v   # expect: FAIL (undefined handleList/defaultListLimit)
```

**Step 3 — impl** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_list.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"context"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

const defaultListLimit = 20

func (s *Server) handleList(_ context.Context, _ *mcp.CallToolRequest, in model.ListInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, model.ListOutput, error) {
	cwd, err := validateCWD(in.CWD)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, model.ListOutput{}, err
	}
	limit := in.Limit
	if limit <= 0 {
		limit = defaultListLimit
	}
	items, err := s.store.ListItems(cwd, limit)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, model.ListOutput{}, err
	}
	if items == nil {
		items = []model.ListItem{}
	}
	return nil, model.ListOutput{Runs: items}, nil
}
```

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestList -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/handler_list*.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: pi_list handler"`

```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestCancel -v   # expect: FAIL
```

**Step 3 — impl** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/handler_cancel.go`:
```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func (s *Server) handleCancel(_ context.Context, _ *mcp.CallToolRequest, in model.CancelInput) (*mcp.CallToolResult, model.CancelOutput, error) {
	if strings.TrimSpace(in.JobID) == "" {
		return nil, model.CancelOutput{}, fmt.Errorf("jobId is required")
	}
	rec, err := s.jobs.Cancel(in.JobID)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, model.CancelOutput{}, err
	}
	return nil, model.CancelOutput{JobID: rec.JobID, Status: string(rec.Status)}, nil
}
```

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestCancel -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/handler_cancel*.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: pi_cancel handler"`

## Task M13 — Tool registration via go-sdk (Register) (test FIRST)

```go
package mcpserver

import (
	"testing"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"
)

func TestRegisterAddsFourTools(t *testing.T) {
	mcpSrv := mcp.NewServer(&mcp.Implementation{Name: "pi-mcp", Version: "v0.1.0"}, nil)
	srv := New(newFakeJobs(), newFakeStore())

	// Register must not panic and must wire all four tools onto the mcp server.
	srv.Register(mcpSrv)

	// Smoke: the registration helper returns the names it registered (for the test + main).
	got := srv.RegisteredToolNames()
	want := map[string]bool{"pi_workflow": false, "pi_status": false, "pi_list": false, "pi_cancel": false}
	for _, n := range got {
		if _, ok := want[n]; ok {
			want[n] = true
		}
	}
	for name, seen := range want {
		if !seen {
			t.Fatalf("tool %q was not registered (got %v)", name, got)
		}
	}
}
```

**Step 2 — run (expect FAIL — undefined Register/RegisteredToolNames):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestRegister -v   # expect: FAIL
```

**Step 3 — impl: append to** `/root/pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver/server.go`:
```go
import (
	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"
)

// Tool descriptions (kept terse; the rich contract lives in the spec/forcing prompt).
const (
	descWorkflow = "Delegate a TASK to the pi dynamic-workflow engine. pi decomposes the task and fans out a heterogeneous fleet of models. Returns immediately with a jobId; poll pi_status. mode=read runs in-place in cwd; mode=write runs in an isolated git worktree and returns branch+diff. Both mode and cwd are REQUIRED."
	descStatus   = "Get live intermediate results and the final synthesized result for a job (by jobId) or run (by runId+cwd). Optional wait=true long-polls until progress or completion."
	descList     = "List recent workflow runs under <cwd>/.pi/workflows/runs (newest first)."
	descCancel   = "Cancel a running job: kill the pi process, mark aborted, and (write mode) prune the worktree/branch."
)

// Register wires all four tools onto the given mcp.Server using the typed generic AddTool.
func (s *Server) Register(m *mcp.Server) {
	mcp.AddTool(m, &mcp.Tool{Name: "pi_workflow", Description: descWorkflow}, s.handleWorkflow)
	mcp.AddTool(m, &mcp.Tool{Name: "pi_status", Description: descStatus}, s.handleStatus)
	mcp.AddTool(m, &mcp.Tool{Name: "pi_list", Description: descList}, s.handleList)
	mcp.AddTool(m, &mcp.Tool{Name: "pi_cancel", Description: descCancel}, s.handleCancel)
}

// RegisteredToolNames reports the tool names Register installs (for main/logging/tests).
func (s *Server) RegisteredToolNames() []string {
	return []string{"pi_workflow", "pi_status", "pi_list", "pi_cancel"}
}
```
> Merge this `mcp` import with the existing `time` import in `server.go` (single import block:
> `"time"` and `"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"`).

**Step 4 — run (expect PASS):**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestRegister -v   # expect: PASS
```

**Step 5 — full-package run + vet:**
```
go test ./internal/mcpserver/... -v   # expect: ALL PASS
go vet ./internal/mcpserver/...       # expect: clean
```

**Step 6 — commit:** `git add internal/mcpserver/server.go internal/mcpserver/server_test.go && git commit -m "mcpserver: register 4 tools via go-sdk AddTool"`

## Task M14 — `cmd/pi-mcp/main.go` wiring (manual smoke; depends on jobs/runstore packages)

> This task wires the concrete `jobs.Registry` and `runstore` into `mcpserver.New` and runs
> the server over stdio. It depends on packages J (jobs) and R (runstore) being built. If their
> concrete method names differ from `JobsService`/`RunStore`, add thin adapter wrappers HERE
> (handlers stay unchanged). No new unit tests — covered by the e2e gate in §10.

**Step 1 — write** `/root/pi-mcp/cmd/pi-mcp/main.go`:
```go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"log"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/jobs"
	"pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver"
	"pi-mcp/internal/runstore"
)

func main() {
	// Concrete dependencies (packages J and R). If their public method names differ from the
	// mcpserver.JobsService / mcpserver.RunStore interfaces, wrap them in small adapters here.
	registry, err := jobs.New() // owns cap-4 pool, persistence, reconciliation on startup
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("jobs init: %v", err)
	}
	store := runstore.New()

	srv := mcpserver.New(registry, store)

	mcpSrv := mcp.NewServer(&mcp.Implementation{Name: "pi-mcp", Version: "v0.1.0"}, nil)
	srv.Register(mcpSrv)
	log.Printf("pi-mcp: registered tools %v", srv.RegisteredToolNames())

	if err := mcpSrv.Run(context.Background(), &mcp.StdioTransport{}); err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("server run: %v", err)
	}
}
```
> If `jobs.New()` / `runstore.New()` have different constructors, adjust the two constructor
> lines to match packages J/R (the contract guarantees the *types* they produce satisfy the
> mcpserver interfaces, directly or via a local adapter).

**Step 2 — build (run where Go is installed and J/R exist):**
```
go build -o /tmp/pi-mcp ./cmd/pi-mcp   # expect: success
```

**Step 3 — manual stdio smoke (optional, requires a built binary):**
```
# initialize handshake — expect a JSON-RPC response listing the 4 tools
printf '%s\n' '{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":1,"method":"tools/list"}' | /tmp/pi-mcp
```

**Step 4 — commit:** `git add cmd/pi-mcp/main.go && git commit -m "pi-mcp: main wires mcpserver over stdio (go-sdk)"`

### Sequencing notes
- M1–M13 are self-contained (depend only on `internal/model` + `internal/config` + go-sdk + fakes).
  They can be implemented before packages J (jobs) and R (runstore) exist.
- M14 (main) is the only task that depends on the concrete J/R packages; sequence it after
  J and R land. The `JobsService`/`RunStore` interfaces in `ports.go` (M1) are the contract J/R
  must satisfy (adapt in main.go if names differ).

### Task IA2 — worktree free-func Prune (path+branch, no Manager)

**Step 1 — failing test** append to `internal/worktree/worktree_test.go`:
```go
func TestFreePrune_RemovesWorktreeAndBranch(t *testing.T) {
    repo := newRepo(t)
    SetBaseDirForTest(t, t.TempDir())
    m, _ := New(ctx(), repo)
    h, _ := m.Create(ctx(), "free1")

    // Free-func Prune, given ONLY path+branch (what jobs stores).
    if err := Prune(ctx(), h.Path, h.Branch); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("free Prune err = %v", err)
    }
    if _, err := os.Stat(h.Path); !os.IsNotExist(err) {
        t.Fatalf("worktree dir still present")
    }
    if exists, _ := m.branchExists(ctx(), h.Branch); exists {
        t.Fatalf("branch %s still present", h.Branch)
    }
}

func TestFreePrune_Idempotent(t *testing.T) {
    repo := newRepo(t)
    SetBaseDirForTest(t, t.TempDir())
    m, _ := New(ctx(), repo)
    h, _ := m.Create(ctx(), "free2")
    if err := Prune(ctx(), h.Path, h.Branch); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("first: %v", err)
    }
    if err := Prune(ctx(), h.Path, h.Branch); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("second (idempotent): %v", err)
    }
}
```

**Step 2 — run (FAIL):** `go test ./internal/worktree/ -run TestFreePrune` → `undefined: Prune`.

**Step 3 — impl** append to `internal/worktree/worktree.go`:
```go
// Prune removes a single worktree + branch given only its path and branch, with no Manager
// (used by jobs cancel/reconcile, which stores only path+branch). It resolves the owning repo
// via the worktree's git-common-dir, then force-removes the worktree, deletes the branch, and
// reaps admin files. Idempotent: missing worktree/branch is not an error.
func Prune(ctx context.Context, worktreePath, branch string) error {
    // Find the main repo dir from the worktree itself.
    common, err := exec.CommandContext(ctx, "git", "-C", worktreePath, "rev-parse", "--git-common-dir").Output()
    repoDir := worktreePath
    if err == nil {
        // git-common-dir is <main>/.git ; its parent is the main worktree.
        repoDir = filepath.Dir(strings.TrimSpace(string(common)))
    }
    run := func(args ...string) {
        _, _ = exec.CommandContext(ctx, "git", append([]string{"-C", repoDir}, args...)...).CombinedOutput()
    }
    run("worktree", "remove", "--force", worktreePath)
    if _, statErr := os.Stat(worktreePath); statErr == nil {
        _ = os.RemoveAll(worktreePath)
    }
    if branch != "" {
        run("branch", "-D", branch)
    }
    run("worktree", "prune")
    return nil
}
```
(Imports: ensure `os/exec`, `path/filepath`, `strings`, `os`, `context` present — merge into the
single existing import group, do not add a second block.)

**Step 4 — run (PASS):** `go test ./internal/worktree/ -run TestFreePrune` → PASS.

**Commit:** `worktree: free-func Prune(ctx,path,branch) for jobs cancel/reconcile (no Manager)`

### Task IA3 — runner-backed Launcher (test with the fake-pi fixture)

**Step 1 — failing test** `internal/app/launcher_test.go`:
```go
package app

import (
    "context"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "testing"
    "time"

    "pi-mcp/internal/config"
    "pi-mcp/internal/jobs"
    "pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

// installFakePi copies the runner's fake pi onto PATH as "pi" and points it at a
// stream fixture that emits a session line + a workflow tool_execution_end(isError:false).
func installFakePi(t *testing.T, fixture string) {
    t.Helper()
    src, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join("..", "runner", "testdata", "fake-pi.sh"))
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("read fake pi: %v", err)
    }
    dir := t.TempDir()
    if err := os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(dir, "pi"), src, 0o755); err != nil {
        t.Fatal(err)
    }
    t.Setenv("PATH", dir+string(os.PathListSeparator)+os.Getenv("PATH"))
    t.Setenv("FAKE_PI_SENTINEL", filepath.Join(dir, "sentinel.out"))
    t.Setenv("FAKE_PI_FIXTURE", fixture)
}

func TestRealLauncher_SuccessSurfacesSessionAndCompletes(t *testing.T) {
    // fixture: a session event + a workflow tool_execution_end isError:false.
    fix := writeFixture(t, ``+
        `{"type":"session","id":"sess-launch-1","cwd":"/tmp"}`+"\n"+
        `{"type":"tool_execution_end","toolName":"workflow","isError":false,`+
        `"result":{"content":[{"type":"text","text":"ok"}]}}`+"\n")
    installFakePi(t, fix)

    pid, sessionCh, wait, err := realLauncher{}.Launch(context.Background(), jobs.Spec{
        Mode: model.ModeRead, CWD: t.TempDir(), Task: "judge", RunsDir: "/x",
    })
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("Launch: %v", err)
    }
    if pid <= 0 {
        t.Fatalf("expected pid, got %d", pid)
    }
    select {
    case sid := <-sessionCh:
        if sid != "sess-launch-1" {
            t.Fatalf("session id = %q, want sess-launch-1", sid)
        }
    case <-time.After(5 * time.Second):
        t.Fatal("no session id within 5s")
    }
    if werr := wait(); werr != nil {
        t.Fatalf("wait should succeed (workflow ok), got %v", werr)
    }
}

func TestRealLauncher_NoWorkflowRun(t *testing.T) {
    fix := writeFixture(t, `{"type":"session","id":"sess-nw"}`+"\n"+`{"type":"agent_end"}`+"\n")
    installFakePi(t, fix)
    _, _, wait, err := realLauncher{}.Launch(context.Background(), jobs.Spec{
        Mode: model.ModeRead, CWD: t.TempDir(), Task: "t",
    })
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("Launch: %v", err)
    }
    if werr := wait(); werr == nil || werr.Error() != config.ErrNoWorkflowRun {
        t.Fatalf("want NO_WORKFLOW_RUN, got %v", werr)
    }
}

func TestRealLauncher_WorkflowIsErrorSurfacesText(t *testing.T) {
    fix := writeFixture(t, ``+
        `{"type":"session","id":"sess-err"}`+"\n"+
        `{"type":"tool_execution_end","toolName":"workflow","isError":true,`+
        `"result":{"content":[{"type":"text","text":"MODEL_ROUTING_ERROR: tier x"}]}}`+"\n")
    installFakePi(t, fix)
    _, _, wait, _ := realLauncher{}.Launch(context.Background(), jobs.Spec{
        Mode: model.ModeRead, CWD: t.TempDir(), Task: "t",
    })
    werr := wait()
    if werr == nil || werr.Error() == "" {
        t.Fatalf("want non-empty isError text, got %v", werr)
    }
}

func writeFixture(t *testing.T, body string) string {
    t.Helper()
    p := filepath.Join(t.TempDir(), "stream.jsonl")
    if err := os.WriteFile(p, []byte(body), 0o644); err != nil {
        t.Fatal(err)
    }
    return p
}
```

**Step 2 — run (FAIL):** `go test ./internal/app/ -run TestRealLauncher` → `undefined: realLauncher`.

**Step 3 — impl** `internal/app/launcher.go` (the `realLauncher` from the contract, plus
`rawErrText(res parser.Result) string` = `strings.TrimSpace(res.RawText)` with a fallback to
`string(res.Result)` then `config.ErrAgentExecutionError`).

**Step 4 — run (PASS):** `go test ./internal/app/ -run TestRealLauncher` → PASS (3 tests).

**Commit:** `app: runner+parser-backed Launcher (session push, NO_WORKFLOW_RUN, isError text)`

### Task IA4 — runstore-backed Correlator

**Step 1 — failing test** `internal/app/correlator_test.go`:
```go
package app

import (
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "testing"

func TestRealCorrelator_FindsRunBySession(t *testing.T) {
    runs := t.TempDir()
    b, _ := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join("..", "runstore", "testdata", "sample-run.json"))

```
(`readSessionID` = decode the file's `sessionId` field with `encoding/json` — small local helper.)

**Step 3 — impl** `internal/app/correlator.go`:
```go
package app

import "pi-mcp/internal/runstore"

type realCorrelator struct{}

func (realCorrelator) RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID string) (string, bool) {
    return runstore.RunIDForSession(runsDir, sessionID)
}
```

**Step 4 — run (PASS).**

**Commit:** `app: runstore-backed Correlator (sessionId -> runId)`

### Task IA5 — worktree-backed Pruner + create-on-submit submit-adapter (mode=write isolation + NOT_A_GIT_REPO)

**Step 1 — failing test** `internal/app/jobs_adapter_test.go`:
```go
package app

import (
    "context"
    "os"
    "os/exec"
    "path/filepath"
    "strings"
    "testing"

    "pi-mcp/internal/config"
    "pi-mcp/internal/jobs"
    "pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver"
    "pi-mcp/internal/model"
)

func gitInitRepo(t *testing.T) string {
    t.Helper()
    dir := t.TempDir()
    for _, args := range [][]string{
        {"init", "-b", "main"}, {"config", "user.email", "t@t"},
        {"config", "user.name", "t"}, {"config", "commit.gpgsign", "false"},
    } {
        c := exec.Command("git", append([]string{"-C", dir}, args...)...)
        if out, err := c.CombinedOutput(); err != nil {
            t.Fatalf("git %v: %v\n%s", args, err, out)
        }
    }
    _ = os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(dir, "README.md"), []byte("hi\n"), 0o644)
    _ = exec.Command("git", "-C", dir, "add", "-A").Run()
    _ = exec.Command("git", "-C", dir, "commit", "-m", "init").Run()
    return dir
}

// newAdapter builds a jobsAdapter whose registry uses the REAL launcher? No — for isolation we
// inject a no-op launcher so Submit returns immediately without spawning pi. We only assert the
// worktree side-effects of create-on-submit.
func newAdapter(t *testing.T) (*jobsAdapter, string) {
    t.Helper()
    base := t.TempDir() // worktree base
    setWorktreeBase(t, base) // calls worktree.SetBaseDirForTest under the hood
    reg := jobs.NewRegistry(jobs.Config{
        Cap: 4, PersistPath: filepath.Join(t.TempDir(), "r.json"), WorktreeRoot: base,
    }, noopLauncher{}, noopCorrelator{}, worktreePruner{})
    return &jobsAdapter{reg: reg, root: base}, base
}

func TestSubmit_WriteCreatesIsolatedWorktree(t *testing.T) {
    a, base := newAdapter(t)
    repo := gitInitRepo(t)
    rec, err := a.Submit(context.Background(), mcpserver.JobSpec{
        Task: "fix", Mode: model.ModeWrite, CWD: repo,
    })
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("Submit write: %v", err)
    }
    if rec.WorktreePath == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(rec.WorktreePath, base) {
        t.Fatalf("worktree not under base: %q (base %q)", rec.WorktreePath, base)
    }
    if strings.HasPrefix(rec.WorktreePath, repo) {
        t.Fatalf("worktree MUST be outside the user repo: %q", rec.WorktreePath)
    }
    if rec.Branch != config.WorktreeBranchPrefix+rec.JobID {
        t.Fatalf("branch = %q, want %s%s", rec.Branch, config.WorktreeBranchPrefix, rec.JobID)
    }
    // RunsDir is inside the worktree (write jobs run there).
    if rec.RunsDir != filepath.Join(rec.WorktreePath, config.RunsDirRel) {
        t.Fatalf("runsDir not in worktree: %q", rec.RunsDir)
    }
    if _, err := os.Stat(rec.WorktreePath); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("worktree dir missing: %v", err)
    }
}

func TestSubmit_WriteNonGitFailsBeforeSpawn(t *testing.T) {
    a, _ := newAdapter(t)
    notRepo := t.TempDir()
    _, err := a.Submit(context.Background(), mcpserver.JobSpec{
        Task: "x", Mode: model.ModeWrite, CWD: notRepo,
    })
    if err == nil || err.Error() != config.ErrNotAGitRepo {
        t.Fatalf("want NOT_A_GIT_REPO before spawn, got %v", err)
    }
}

func TestSubmit_ReadNoWorktree(t *testing.T) {
    a, _ := newAdapter(t)
    rec, err := a.Submit(context.Background(), mcpserver.JobSpec{
        Task: "scan", Mode: model.ModeRead, CWD: t.TempDir(),
    })
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("Submit read: %v", err)
    }
    if rec.WorktreePath != "" {
        t.Fatalf("read mode must have no worktree, got %q", rec.WorktreePath)
    }
}
```
Add tiny test doubles in the same file:
```go
type noopLauncher struct{}
func (noopLauncher) Launch(ctx context.Context, s jobs.Spec) (int, <-chan string, func() error, error) {
    ch := make(chan string); close(ch)
    return 1, ch, func() error { return nil }, nil
}
type noopCorrelator struct{}
func (noopCorrelator) RunIDForSession(string, string) (string, bool) { return "", false }
```
`setWorktreeBase(t, base)` calls `worktree.SetBaseDirForTest(t, base)` (W package's existing seam).

**Step 2 — run (FAIL):** `go test ./internal/app/ -run TestSubmit` → `undefined: jobsAdapter`,
`worktreePruner`, etc.

**Step 3 — impl** `internal/app/jobs_adapter.go` (the `jobsAdapter`, `worktreePruner`,
`newJobID`, and the `remember/handle` map for WriteInfoFor — full shapes in the contract).
`jobs.Spec` gains `PreassignedID` and `Task`/`Context` (see edits); `NewJob` honors them.

**Step 4 — run (PASS):** `go test ./internal/app/ -run TestSubmit` → PASS (3 tests).

**Commit:** `app: jobsAdapter create-on-submit worktree isolation + NOT_A_GIT_REPO + worktreePruner`

```go
package app

import (
```

```go
func TestWriteInfoFor_NonEmptyDiff(t *testing.T) {
    a, _ := newAdapter(t)
    repo := gitInitRepo(t)
    rec, err := a.Submit(context.Background(), mcpserver.JobSpec{
        Task: "edit", Mode: model.ModeWrite, CWD: repo,
    })
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("Submit: %v", err)

    _ = os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(rec.WorktreePath, "new.txt"), []byte("new\n"), 0o644)
    _ = exec.Command("git", "-C", rec.WorktreePath, "add", "-A").Run() // stage so files_changed sees new file

    wi, ok := a.WriteInfoFor(rec.JobID)
    if !ok {
        t.Fatal("WriteInfoFor ok=false, want true for a write job")
    }
    if wi.Branch != rec.Branch || wi.WorktreePath != rec.WorktreePath {
        t.Fatalf("write info identity wrong: %+v", wi)
    }
    if wi.DiffStat == "" {
        t.Fatalf("diff_stat must be non-empty after edits")
    }
    if len(wi.FilesChanged) == 0 {
        t.Fatalf("files_changed must be non-empty after edits")
    }
}

    })

        t.Fatal("read job must have WriteInfoFor ok=false")
    }
}
```

### Task IA8 — §9 error threading into pi_status (JobRecord.ErrorMessage first)

```go
func TestStatus_FailureMessagePrefersRecordErrorMessage(t *testing.T) {
    run := buildRun()
    run.Status = "failed"
    run.Result = nil
    run.Logs = []string{"run-xyz log line"}            // #3
    run.Agents[0].Status = "error"
    em := "agent boom"
    run.Agents[0].Error = &em                          // #2
    j := newFakeJobs()
    j.lookup["job-f"] = model.JobRecord{
        JobID: "job-f", RunsDir: "/runs", RunID: run.RunID, PID: 1, Status: model.JobFailed,
        ErrorMessage: "WORKFLOW isError text", ErrorCode: config.ErrAgentExecutionError, // #1
    }
    store := newFakeStore()
    store.runs["/runs/"+run.RunID] = run
    srv := New(j, store)
    _, out, _ := srv.handleStatus(ctxBG(), nil, model.StatusInput{JobID: "job-f"})
    if out.Error != "WORKFLOW isError text" {
        t.Fatalf("want #1 record ErrorMessage, got %q", out.Error)
    }
}

func TestStatus_FailureMessageFallsBackToAgentThenLogs(t *testing.T) {
    run := buildRun()
    run.Status = "failed"
    run.Result = nil
    run.Logs = []string{"run-xyz log line"}
    em := "agent boom"
    run.Agents[0].Status = "error"
    run.Agents[0].Error = &em
    j := newFakeJobs()
    j.lookup["job-g"] = model.JobRecord{JobID: "job-g", RunsDir: "/runs", RunID: run.RunID,
        PID: 1, Status: model.JobFailed} // no ErrorMessage -> #2 wins
    store := newFakeStore()
    store.runs["/runs/"+run.RunID] = run
    srv := New(j, store)
    _, out, _ := srv.handleStatus(ctxBG(), nil, model.StatusInput{JobID: "job-g"})
    if out.Error != "agent boom" {
        t.Fatalf("want #2 agent error, got %q", out.Error)
    }
}
```

**Step 2 — run (FAIL):** `go test ./internal/mcpserver/ -run TestStatus_FailureMessage`
(fails: current `failureMessage` ignores the record).

- add `errorMessage string` + `errorCode string` to `resolved`; populate from the looked-up
  record in `resolveTarget` (both jobId and runId paths).
- change `failureMessage(run)` → `failureMessage(recMsg string, run *model.Run)` per the contract
  and call it as `out.Error = failureMessage(tgt.errorMessage, run)`.

```go
package app

import (
    "bytes"

    "strings"

func TestRun_ReconcileThenServe(t *testing.T) {
    var buf bytes.Buffer
    logger := log.New(&buf, "", 0)
    reg := jobs.NewRegistry(jobs.Config{Cap: 4, PersistPath: t.TempDir() + "/r.json"},
        noopLauncher{}, noopCorrelator{}, worktreePruner{})

    served := false
    d := Deps{
        Logger:        logger,
        buildRegistry: func(Deps) (*jobs.Registry, error) { return reg, nil },
        newServer:     func() *mcp.Server { return mcp.NewServer(&mcp.Implementation{Name: "t"}, nil) },

    }

        t.Fatal("serve was not called")

    }

}
```

## cmd/pi-mcp wiring + startup reconciliation, MCP e2e smoke (PI_MCP_E2E), Fase-0 fixtures, go vet/build, install/registration (`main_e2e`)

**Files:** /root/pi-mcp/cmd/pi-mcp/main.go, /root/pi-mcp/cmd/pi-mcp/main_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/app/app.go, /root/pi-mcp/internal/app/app_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/test/e2e/e2e_smoke_test.go, /root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl, /root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-partial.json, /root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh, /root/pi-mcp/go.mod, /root/pi-mcp/go.sum

_Assumptions:_ Go is NOT installed in this build env (verified-by-foundation: `go version` not found, no SDK in /root/go/pkg/mod). Every `go`/`pi`/`claude` command is written to run where those tools exist; Task Z1 gates on `go version`.; DOWNSTREAM SEAM (negotiated, not in the frozen contract): package `internal/jobs` exposes `func New(ctx context.Context, opts jobs.Options) (*jobs.Registry, error)` where `Options` has at least `Logger *log.Logger` and `ConcurrencyCap int`; `*jobs.Registry` has `Reconcile(ctx context.Context) (int, error)` and `Close() error`. If the real package B differs, only `internal/app/app.go`'s `newRegistryReal` adapter changes — the wiring logic + its table test are seam-isolated and stay valid.; DOWNSTREAM SEAM: package `internal/mcpserver` exposes `func Register(s *mcp.Server, reg *jobs.Registry) error` that calls `mcp.AddTool` for the 4 tools (pi_workflow/pi_status/pi_list/pi_cancel) using the model I/O structs. If B/C's real signatures differ, only `registerReal` in `internal/app/app.go` changes.; I introduced `internal/app` (not named in spec §6) purely as a testable wiring seam so `main.go` stays a 3-line delegate and the startup sequence (build registry -> reconcile -> register -> serve) is unit-testable with fakes without spawning real `pi`. This is additive and does not alter any frozen type/signature.; go-sdk CLIENT-side symbols used in the e2e (mcp.NewClient, mcp.CommandTransport, session.CallTool, mcp.CallToolParams, CallToolResult.StructuredContent, mcp.TextContent) are assumed from the same SDK family as the verified server-side API; they are not in the frozen server-side notes. Verify against the pinned SDK version in go.mod before the first e2e run; if names differ, fix only decodeStructured/the transport line.; Server Implementation is Name:"pi-mcp", Version:"v0.1.0" per the verified contract; the e2e client uses its own Implementation name.; Fase-0 fixtures (sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl, sample-run-partial.json) are best captured from a real `pi` via scripts/capture-fixtures.sh; when `pi`/the fork trigger is unavailable, the tasks give exact hand-authoring instructions derived by trimming the existing sample-run.json / sample event stream. The binding PASS gate for these fixtures lives in the parser/runstore/jobs package tests, not this package.; The e2e test treats `status=failed` + `error=NO_WORKFLOW_RUN` as a documented SKIP (un-forked pi, spec §9), not a failure — so the suite is green on hosts without the fork while still being a real assertion when the fork is present.; Logs go to stderr only; stdout is the MCP stdio transport and must never be written to by app code (standard MCP-over-stdio rule).; Work happens on branch feat/main-e2e; commits are listed per task but only performed when the user/orchestrator asks to commit per the environment's git policy.

# Package Z — main_e2e: `cmd/pi-mcp` wiring, startup reconciliation, MCP e2e smoke, Fase-0 fixtures, vet/build, install

This package is the integration seam. It depends on the other packages' exported constructors:
- `config` (package A): consts (`PiBinary`, `DefaultConcurrencyCap`, `StaleThreshold`, `RunsDirRel`, ...).
- `jobs` (package B/registry): a `Registry` with `New(...)` + `Reconcile(ctx) (reconciled int, err error)` + `Close() error`.
- `mcpserver` (package C): a `Register(server *mcp.Server, reg *jobs.Registry)` that wires the 4 tools onto a go-sdk `*mcp.Server`.

Because the exact downstream constructor signatures are NOT in the frozen foundation contract (only the model/config types are), this package defines a **thin, narrow seam interface** in `internal/app` so `main.go` and the wiring are fully testable WITHOUT importing the heavy job-runner. See assumptions for the exact seam. If a downstream package's real constructor differs, only `cmd/pi-mcp/main.go`'s constructor call and the `internal/app` adapter need touching — the wiring/reconciliation logic and its tests stay valid.

> **Go is not installed in this build env** (`go version` → not found; no SDK in `/root/go/pkg/mod`). Every `go` command below is written to run **where Go 1.23+ is installed**. Task Z1 starts with a Go-presence check. Do NOT mark a "run" step green from this env — it is the implementer's gate on a Go-capable machine.

> Tasks are numbered Z1.. so they can be re-sequenced. Each task: failing test → run (exact cmd + expected FAIL) → minimal complete impl → run (expected PASS) → commit. Work on a branch `feat/main-e2e`, never on `master`.

---

## Task Z1 — Go-presence check + module + `cmd/pi-mcp/main.go` skeleton builds

```

```

**Step Z1.3 — write the minimal `main.go` (complete code).**
Create `/root/pi-mcp/cmd/pi-mcp/main.go`:
```go
// Command pi-mcp is the MCP server entrypoint. It wires config + the job
// registry + the MCP tool handlers and serves them over stdio (go-sdk).
package main

import (
	"context"
	"log"
	"os"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/app"
)

func main() {
	// Logs go to stderr only. stdout is the MCP transport — never write to it.
	logger := log.New(os.Stderr, "pi-mcp ", log.LstdFlags|log.Lmsgprefix)

	if err := app.Run(context.Background(), app.Deps{Logger: logger}); err != nil {
		logger.Fatalf("fatal: %v", err)
	}
}
```

**Step Z1.4 — run (expected FAIL: `internal/app` does not exist yet).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go build ./cmd/pi-mcp
```
Expected FAIL: `package pi-mcp/internal/app is not in std ... cannot find module`. This proves `main.go` parses and the only missing piece is the seam, built next.

**Commit:** `git -C /root/pi-mcp add cmd/pi-mcp/main.go go.mod go.sum && git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -m "Z1: pi-mcp main entrypoint skeleton (delegates to internal/app)"`

## Task Z2 — `internal/app`: the wiring seam + startup reconciliation (table-driven test FIRST)

The `app` package owns: construct logger-aware deps → build registry → **run startup reconciliation** (GC of orphan `pi-mcp/job-*` worktrees + mark stale/terminal jobs) → register the 4 tools on an `*mcp.Server` → serve over `&mcp.StdioTransport{}` until the client disconnects. Reconciliation must be **graceful**: a reconcile error is logged (stderr) and startup CONTINUES (a recoverable disk-scan failure must not stop the server from serving fresh jobs).

**Step Z2.1 — failing test for the seam ordering + graceful reconcile.**
Create `/root/pi-mcp/internal/app/app_test.go`:
```go
package app

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"errors"
	"log"
	"strings"
	"testing"
)

// fakeRegistry records the order of lifecycle calls and lets a test inject
// a reconcile error / count.
type fakeRegistry struct {
	reconcileN   int
	reconcileErr error
	calls        []string
}

func (f *fakeRegistry) Reconcile(ctx context.Context) (int, error) {
	f.calls = append(f.calls, "reconcile")
	return f.reconcileN, f.reconcileErr
}
func (f *fakeRegistry) Close() error {
	f.calls = append(f.calls, "close")
	return nil
}

func TestStartup_ReconcileThenServe(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name        string
		reg         *fakeRegistry
		registerErr error
		serveErr    error
		wantErr     bool
		wantLog     string // substring expected in stderr log
		wantCalls   []string
	}{
		{
			name:      "happy path reconciles then serves then closes",
			reg:       &fakeRegistry{reconcileN: 2},
			wantErr:   false,
			wantLog:   "reconciled 2",
			wantCalls: []string{"reconcile", "close"},
		},
		{
			name:      "reconcile error is logged but startup continues",
			reg:       &fakeRegistry{reconcileErr: errors.New("disk scan boom")},
			wantErr:   false,
			wantLog:   "reconcile error: disk scan boom",
			wantCalls: []string{"reconcile", "close"},
		},
		{
			name:        "register error aborts before serving (no swallow)",
			reg:         &fakeRegistry{},
			registerErr: errors.New("bad tool"),
			wantErr:     true,
			wantCalls:   []string{"reconcile", "close"},
		},
		{
			name:      "serve error is returned to caller",
			reg:       &fakeRegistry{},
			serveErr:  errors.New("transport closed unexpectedly"),
			wantErr:   true,
			wantCalls: []string{"reconcile", "close"},
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range tests {
		t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf bytes.Buffer
			logger := log.New(&buf, "", 0)

			served := false
			d := Deps{
				Logger: logger,
				newRegistry: func(ctx context.Context, l *log.Logger) (registry, error) {
					return tc.reg, nil
				},
				register: func(srv server, r registry) error {
					return tc.registerErr
				},
				serve: func(ctx context.Context, srv server) error {
					served = true
					return tc.serveErr
				},
				newServer: func() server { return stubServer{} },
			}

			err := Run(context.Background(), d)

			if tc.wantErr && err == nil {
				t.Fatalf("want error, got nil")
			}
			if !tc.wantErr && err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("want no error, got %v", err)
			}
			if tc.registerErr != nil && served {
				t.Fatalf("serve must NOT run when register fails")
			}
			if tc.wantLog != "" && !strings.Contains(buf.String(), tc.wantLog) {
				t.Fatalf("log %q missing substring %q", buf.String(), tc.wantLog)
			}
			gotCalls := strings.Join(tc.reg.calls, ",")
			wantCalls := strings.Join(tc.wantCalls, ",")
			if gotCalls != wantCalls {
				t.Fatalf("lifecycle calls = %q, want %q", gotCalls, wantCalls)
			}
		})
	}
}

type stubServer struct{}

func (stubServer) marker() {}
```

**Step Z2.2 — run (expected FAIL: package `app` does not compile, undefined symbols).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go test ./internal/app/
```
Expected FAIL: `undefined: Deps`, `undefined: Run`, `undefined: registry`, `undefined: server`, etc. (red — no impl).

**Step Z2.3 — minimal complete impl of the seam.**
Create `/root/pi-mcp/internal/app/app.go`:
```go
// Package app wires config + the job registry + the MCP tool handlers and
// serves them over stdio. It is split out of main so the startup sequence
// (build registry -> reconcile -> register tools -> serve) is unit-testable
// with fakes, without spawning the real pi subprocess.
package app

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"

	"pi-mcp/internal/config"
	"pi-mcp/internal/jobs"
	"pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver"
)

// registry is the narrow seam the app needs from the job registry. The real
// *jobs.Registry satisfies it; tests inject a fake.
type registry interface {
	// Reconcile scans the persisted registry + pi-mcp/job-* worktrees, marks
	// stale/terminal jobs, and GCs orphans. Returns how many records it
	// reconciled. A non-nil error is recoverable (logged, startup continues).
	Reconcile(ctx context.Context) (int, error)
	Close() error
}

// server is the narrow seam the app needs from the MCP server. The real
// *mcp.Server satisfies it via the adapter in newServerReal.
type server interface{ marker() }

// Deps carries collaborators. The function fields are unexported seams that
// default (via fill) to the real implementations; tests override them.
type Deps struct {
	Logger *log.Logger

	newRegistry func(ctx context.Context, l *log.Logger) (registry, error)
	register    func(srv server, r registry) error
	serve       func(ctx context.Context, srv server) error
	newServer   func() server
}

// Run executes the full startup sequence and blocks in serve until the MCP
// client disconnects. Reconciliation failures are logged but do not abort
// startup; register/serve failures are returned.
func Run(ctx context.Context, d Deps) error {
	d = fill(d)

	reg, err := d.newRegistry(ctx, d.Logger)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("build registry: %w", err)
	}
	defer func() { _ = reg.Close() }()

	// Graceful startup reconciliation (spec §8): mark stale/terminal jobs and
	// GC orphan worktrees. A disk-scan error must not stop us from serving.
	n, rerr := reg.Reconcile(ctx)
	if rerr != nil {
		d.Logger.Printf("startup reconcile error: %v (continuing)", rerr)
	} else {
		d.Logger.Printf("startup reconciled %d job record(s)", n)
	}

	srv := d.newServer()
	if err := d.register(srv, reg); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("register tools: %w", err)
	}

	d.Logger.Printf("serving %q %s over stdio", config.PiBinary+"-mcp", "v0.1.0")
	if err := d.serve(ctx, srv); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("serve: %w", err)
	}
	return nil
}

// fill installs the real implementations for any seam the caller left nil.
func fill(d Deps) Deps {
	if d.Logger == nil {
		d.Logger = log.Default()
	}
	if d.newRegistry == nil {
		d.newRegistry = newRegistryReal
	}
	if d.newServer == nil {
		d.newServer = newServerReal
	}
	if d.register == nil {
		d.register = registerReal
	}
	if d.serve == nil {
		d.serve = serveReal
	}
	return d
}

// realServer adapts *mcp.Server to the server seam.
type realServer struct{ s *mcp.Server }

func (realServer) marker() {}

func newServerReal() server {
	return realServer{s: mcp.NewServer(
		&mcp.Implementation{Name: "pi-mcp", Version: "v0.1.0"}, nil)}
}

func newRegistryReal(ctx context.Context, l *log.Logger) (registry, error) {
	return jobs.New(ctx, jobs.Options{
		Logger:         l,
		ConcurrencyCap: config.DefaultConcurrencyCap,
	})
}

func registerReal(srv server, r registry) error {
	rs, ok := srv.(realServer)
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Errorf("register: unexpected server type %T", srv)
	}
	reg, ok := r.(*jobs.Registry)
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Errorf("register: unexpected registry type %T", r)
	}
	return mcpserver.Register(rs.s, reg)
}

func serveReal(ctx context.Context, srv server) error {
	rs, ok := srv.(realServer)
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Errorf("serve: unexpected server type %T", srv)
	}
	return rs.s.Run(ctx, &mcp.StdioTransport{})
}
```

**Step Z2.4 — run (expected PASS for app_test, but `registerReal`/`newRegistryReal` reference jobs/mcpserver which may not exist yet).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go test ./internal/app/
```
Expected: the **unit test PASSES** because it overrides every seam (`newRegistry`, `register`, `serve`, `newServer`) and never touches the real adapters. BUT compilation of `app.go` requires `pi-mcp/internal/jobs` (with `jobs.New`, `jobs.Options{Logger,ConcurrencyCap}`, `*jobs.Registry`) and `pi-mcp/internal/mcpserver` (with `mcpserver.Register`) to exist. If those packages are not yet built by packages B/C, this step is **blocked on them** — see the integration gate note below. To unblock unit work independently, temporarily stub them (delete stub before final integration). Document the dependency, do not invent the real bodies here.

> **Integration gate:** Z2.4 only goes green once packages `jobs` and `mcpserver` expose the seam in the assumptions. Until then the *test* logic is verified via the seam overrides; the *adapters* are compile-checked against the real packages at integration time (Task Z7).

**Commit (once green):** `git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -am "Z2: internal/app startup wiring + graceful reconciliation (table-driven seam test)"`
