## Task Z4 — Fase-0 fixture generation: capture `sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl`

Per spec §10/§11, two fixtures must be captured from REAL `pi` runs:
1. `sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl` — a `pi -p --mode json` stream where the model **answers directly** (no `tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow")`), used by the parser's NEGATIVE test (`→ NO_WORKFLOW_RUN`).
2. `sample-run-partial.json` — a mid-flight run file (Task Z5).

This task captures #1 with a deterministic capture script so it is reproducible (and re-runnable when the fork's behavior changes).

**Step Z4.1 — write the capture script.**
Create `/root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh`:
```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Fase-0 fixture capture (spec §11). Requires a working `pi` on PATH and the
# same env Claude Code would pass (AGENT_VAULT_*, HOME, PATH). NOT run in CI —
# run once on a machine with pi configured, then commit the trimmed outputs.
set -euo pipefail

FIX="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")/.." && pwd)/docs/research/fixtures"
mkdir -p "$FIX"

# --- (1) sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl ---------------------------------------
# A prompt that pi can answer DIRECTLY (no workflow tool call). We deliberately
# DO NOT send the forcing prompt here. Expect: a session line + text/turn
# events + agent_end, but NO tool_execution_end(toolName="workflow").
echo "capturing sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl ..."
pi -p --mode json --no-session "What is 2 + 2? Answer with just the number, no tools." \
  < /dev/null \
  > "$FIX/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl"

# Sanity: assert the negative property holds before committing.
if grep -q '"toolName":"workflow"' "$FIX/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl"; then
  echo "FATAL: capture contains a workflow tool call; not a NO_WORKFLOW fixture" >&2
  exit 1
fi
if ! grep -q '"type":"session"' "$FIX/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl"; then
  echo "FATAL: capture missing session event" >&2
  exit 1
fi
echo "ok: sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl ($(wc -l < "$FIX/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl") lines)"

echo "Done. Review, trim if huge, then: git add docs/research/fixtures/ && git commit"
```

**Step Z4.2 — make executable + run capture (where `pi` exists).**
```
chmod +x /root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh
/root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh
```
Expected: prints `ok: sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl (N lines)`. The script's own asserts are the test: it FAILS loudly if the capture accidentally contains a workflow tool call or lacks a session event. If `pi` is unavailable, hand-author a minimal fixture matching the contract: a `{"type":"session",...}` line, one `{"type":"text",...}` answer line, a `{"type":"turn_end",...}`, and a final `{"type":"agent_end",...}` — and crucially **no** `tool_execution_end` with `"toolName":"workflow"`.

**Step Z4.3 — verify fixture shape (the assertion = the test).**
```
test "$(grep -c '"toolName":"workflow"' /root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl)" = "0" \
  && grep -q '"type":"session"' /root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl \
  && echo NEGATIVE_FIXTURE_OK
```
Expected: `NEGATIVE_FIXTURE_OK`. This fixture is consumed by **package parser's** negative test — that package's test (`→ NO_WORKFLOW_RUN`) is the real PASS gate; coordinate so it reads this file.

**Commit:** `git -C /root/pi-mcp add scripts/capture-fixtures.sh docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl && git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -m "Z4: Fase-0 capture script + sample-run-no-workflow.jsonl negative fixture"`

---

## Task Z5 — Fase-0 fixture generation: capture/author `sample-run-partial.json`

Per spec §10, a mid-flight run file: `status=running` (+ a `paused` variant), journal subset **out of order** (e.g. index 0,2), agents mixed `done`/`running`, and `result`/`tokenUsage`/`completedAt`/`durationMs` **OMITTED**. Used by runstore + jobs long-poll tests.

**Step Z5.1 — add the partial capture to the script (snapshot during a live run).**
Append to `/root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh` (before the final `echo Done`):
```bash
# --- (2) sample-run-partial.json --------------------------------------------
# Snapshot the run file MID-FLIGHT. Launch a forced workflow in the background,
# poll for the run file to appear, copy it the instant journal has a partial
# (>=1 but < agentCount) set of entries, then kill pi.
echo "capturing sample-run-partial.json ..."
WORKDIR="$(mktemp -d)"
( cd "$WORKDIR" && git init -q . )
PROMPT="$(cat "$FIX/sample-forced-workflow-prompt.txt")"
( cd "$WORKDIR" && pi -p --mode json --no-session "$PROMPT" < /dev/null > /dev/null 2>&1 ) &
PI_PID=$!
RUNS="$WORKDIR/.pi/workflows/runs"
# Wait up to 60s for a run file with a partial journal.
for _ in $(seq 1 600); do
  f="$(ls -1 "$RUNS"/*.json 2>/dev/null | head -1 || true)"
  if [ -n "${f:-}" ]; then
    n="$(grep -o '"index"' "$f" | wc -l || echo 0)"
    if [ "$n" -ge 1 ] && [ "$n" -lt 4 ]; then
      cp "$f" "$FIX/sample-run-partial.json"
      break
    fi
  fi
  sleep 0.1
done
kill "$PI_PID" 2>/dev/null || true
wait "$PI_PID" 2>/dev/null || true
rm -rf "$WORKDIR"
test -f "$FIX/sample-run-partial.json" || { echo "FATAL: no partial captured" >&2; exit 1; }
echo "ok: sample-run-partial.json"
```

**Step Z5.2 — run the capture (where `pi` exists + fork trigger wired).**
```
/root/pi-mcp/scripts/capture-fixtures.sh
```
Expected: `ok: sample-run-partial.json`. Race-sensitive — re-run if it grabbed a full journal. If `pi`/fork unavailable, **hand-author** `/root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-partial.json` by trimming `sample-run.json`: keep `runId/sessionId/workflowName/script/currentPhase/phases/logs`, set `"status":"running"`, keep `journal` entries for **index 0 and 2 only** (out of order), set the 4 `agents[]` to mixed statuses (callIndex 0/2 `done`, 1/3 `running`), and **delete** `result`, `tokenUsage`, `completedAt`, `durationMs`. Add a sibling `sample-run-partial-paused.json` identical but `"status":"paused"` for the running↔paused test.

**Step Z5.3 — verify shape (assertion = test).**
```
python3 - <<'PY'
import json
d=json.load(open("/root/pi-mcp/docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-partial.json"))
assert d["status"] in ("running","paused"), d["status"]
idx=[j["index"] for j in d["journal"]]
assert 0 < len(idx) < 4, idx
assert idx != sorted(idx) or len(idx)<len(d["agents"]), "journal must be a partial/out-of-order subset"
for k in ("result","tokenUsage","completedAt","durationMs"):
    assert k not in d or d[k] in (None,""), f"{k} must be omitted while running"
print("PARTIAL_FIXTURE_OK", idx)
PY
```
Expected: `PARTIAL_FIXTURE_OK [0, 2]` (or similar partial out-of-order set). This fixture is consumed by **runstore + jobs** tests — those packages' tests are the binding PASS gate.

**Commit:** `git -C /root/pi-mcp add scripts/capture-fixtures.sh docs/research/fixtures/sample-run-partial.json && git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -m "Z5: Fase-0 sample-run-partial.json mid-flight fixture + capture step"`

---

## Task Z6 — Real MCP e2e smoke (gated by `PI_MCP_E2E=1`)

Per spec §10: a go-sdk MCP **client** spawns `pi-mcp` over stdio → calls `pi_workflow{mode:read}` → polls `pi_status{wait:true}` until `completed` → asserts multi-model fan-out (`by_model` has ≥2 distinct models, `agentCount`≥2). Gated off by default; **requires the forked headless trigger** else `NO_WORKFLOW_RUN` (the test documents and tolerates that distinctly).

**Step Z6.1 — write the gated e2e test.**
Create `/root/pi-mcp/test/e2e/e2e_smoke_test.go`:
```go
package e2e

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk/mcp"
)

// TestE2E_WorkflowReadFanout is a real end-to-end smoke: it builds the
// pi-mcp binary, launches it as an MCP server over stdio via the go-sdk
// client transport, drives pi_workflow{mode:read} and polls pi_status{wait}
// to a terminal state, then asserts a multi-model fan-out.
//
// GATED: only runs with PI_MCP_E2E=1 AND a `pi` whose fork actually triggers
// the headless workflow. Without the fork trigger the run returns
// NO_WORKFLOW_RUN (spec §9) and the test reports that as a SKIP-with-reason,
// because that is the documented, expected outcome of an un-forked pi.
func TestE2E_WorkflowReadFanout(t *testing.T) {
	if os.Getenv("PI_MCP_E2E") != "1" {
		t.Skip("set PI_MCP_E2E=1 (and a fork-triggered pi on PATH) to run the e2e smoke")
	}

	bin := buildBinary(t)

	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Minute)
	defer cancel()

	client := mcp.NewClient(&mcp.Implementation{Name: "pi-mcp-e2e", Version: "v0.0.0"}, nil)
	cmd := exec.CommandContext(ctx, bin)
	cmd.Env = os.Environ() // passthrough AGENT_VAULT_*, HOME, PATH (spec §13)
	cmd.Stderr = os.Stderr
	session, err := client.Connect(ctx, &mcp.CommandTransport{Command: cmd}, nil)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("connect to pi-mcp: %v", err)
	}
	defer session.Close()

	cwd, _ := os.Getwd()

	// 1) Kick off a read-mode workflow.
	startRes, err := session.CallTool(ctx, &mcp.CallToolParams{
		Name: "pi_workflow",
		Arguments: map[string]any{
			"task": "Judge each: (A) Earth orbits the Sun; (B) water boils at 10C at sea level; (C) 7 is prime. Give a verdict and one-line overall.",
			"mode": "read",
			"cwd":  cwd,
		},
	})
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("pi_workflow call: %v", err)
	}
	var start struct {
		JobID  string `json:"jobId"`
		Status string `json:"status"`
	}
	decodeStructured(t, startRes, &start)
	if start.JobID == "" {
		t.Fatalf("pi_workflow returned empty jobId: %+v", start)
	}
	t.Logf("started jobId=%s status=%s", start.JobID, start.Status)

	// 2) Poll pi_status{wait:true} until terminal.
	var last struct {
		Status   string `json:"status"`
		Error    string `json:"error"`
		Metadata struct {
			ByModel    map[string]int `json:"by_model"`
			AgentCount int            `json:"agentCount"`
		} `json:"metadata"`
	}
	deadline := time.Now().Add(4 * time.Minute)
	for time.Now().Before(deadline) {
		stRes, err := session.CallTool(ctx, &mcp.CallToolParams{
			Name:      "pi_status",
			Arguments: map[string]any{"jobId": start.JobID, "wait": true},
		})
		if err != nil {
			t.Fatalf("pi_status call: %v", err)
		}
		decodeStructured(t, stRes, &last)
		t.Logf("status=%s agents=%d models=%v err=%q",
			last.Status, last.Metadata.AgentCount, last.Metadata.ByModel, last.Error)
		switch last.Status {
		case "completed", "failed", "aborted":
			goto done
		}
	}
done:
	// Documented expected outcome without the fork: NO_WORKFLOW_RUN.
	if last.Status == "failed" && last.Error == "NO_WORKFLOW_RUN" {
		t.Skipf("pi did not trigger a workflow (NO_WORKFLOW_RUN) — needs the forked headless trigger (spec §9)")
	}
	if last.Status != "completed" {
		t.Fatalf("workflow did not complete: status=%s error=%q", last.Status, last.Error)
	}
	if last.Metadata.AgentCount < 2 {
		t.Fatalf("expected fan-out (>=2 agents), got %d", last.Metadata.AgentCount)
	}
	if len(last.Metadata.ByModel) < 2 {
		t.Fatalf("expected multi-model fan-out (>=2 distinct models), got %v", last.Metadata.ByModel)
	}
	t.Logf("E2E PASS: %d agents across %d models %v",
		last.Metadata.AgentCount, len(last.Metadata.ByModel), last.Metadata.ByModel)
}

func buildBinary(t *testing.T) string {
	t.Helper()
	bin := t.TempDir() + "/pi-mcp"
	cmd := exec.Command("go", "build", "-o", bin, "../../cmd/pi-mcp")
	cmd.Stderr = os.Stderr
	if err := cmd.Run(); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("go build pi-mcp: %v", err)
	}
	return bin
}

// decodeStructured pulls the tool's structured output. The go-sdk surfaces the
// typed Output as StructuredContent (a Go value) on the result; we round-trip
// through JSON into the caller's target.
func decodeStructured(t *testing.T, res *mcp.CallToolResult, target any) {
	t.Helper()
	if res.IsError {
		// Surface the text content for diagnosis.
		for _, c := range res.Content {
			if tc, ok := c.(*mcp.TextContent); ok {
				t.Logf("tool error content: %s", tc.Text)
			}
		}
	}
	b, err := json.Marshal(res.StructuredContent)
	if err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("marshal structured content: %v", err)
	}
	if err := json.Unmarshal(b, target); err != nil {
		t.Fatalf("unmarshal structured content %s: %v", string(b), err)
	}
}
```

**Step Z6.2 — run gated OFF (expected: SKIP, proves it compiles + is correctly gated).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go test ./test/e2e/
```
Expected: `ok  pi-mcp/test/e2e  (cached) ... --- SKIP: TestE2E_WorkflowReadFanout (set PI_MCP_E2E=1 ...)`. Green via skip — confirms the client/transport API compiles against the go-sdk and the binary builds. (Requires `internal/app`+deps to compile, i.e. integration gate.)

**Step Z6.3 — run gated ON, on a fork-enabled host (the real e2e).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && PI_MCP_E2E=1 go test -count=1 -timeout=10m -v ./test/e2e/
```
Expected (forked pi): logs `started jobId=...`, polls to `status=completed`, asserts `agentCount>=2` and `>=2` distinct models (matching the validated `{flash:3, gpt-5.5:1}` shape from §3), prints `E2E PASS`. Without the fork trigger: SKIP with reason `NO_WORKFLOW_RUN`. A hard FAIL means the wiring is wrong (connection, tool names, or status mapping).

> Note: `mcp.CommandTransport`, `mcp.NewClient`, `session.CallTool`, `CallToolParams`, `CallToolResult.StructuredContent`, and `mcp.TextContent` are the client-side go-sdk symbols. If the installed SDK version names any of these differently, fix only `decodeStructured`/the transport line — the test flow is contract-stable. Verify against the pinned SDK in `go.mod` before first run.

**Commit:** `git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -am "Z6: real MCP e2e smoke (PI_MCP_E2E gated): pi_workflow read -> poll pi_status{wait} -> assert multi-model fan-out"`

---

## Task Z7 — Integration: `go vet` + `go build` + full `go test ./...` (the binding gate)

This task is the cross-package integration gate. It only goes fully green once packages A (config), B (jobs), and C (mcpserver) are merged and expose the seam in the assumptions.

**Step Z7.1 — vet (static checks across all packages).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go vet ./...
```
Expected: no output, exit 0. Fix any vet finding (printf mismatches, unkeyed struct literals, etc.) before proceeding.

**Step Z7.2 — build the binary.**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go build -o ./bin/pi-mcp ./cmd/pi-mcp && ./bin/pi-mcp --help 2>&1 | head -1 || true
```
Expected: builds with no errors; `./bin/pi-mcp` exists. (`--help` is not implemented — the server reads stdio; a non-crash/EOF is fine. Do NOT leave the server running; it blocks on stdin.) `bin/` is gitignored.

**Step Z7.3 — full test suite (unit; e2e stays skipped).**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go test ./...
```
Expected: every package `ok`, e2e `SKIP`. If `internal/app` adapters fail to compile, the real `jobs.New(ctx, jobs.Options{Logger,ConcurrencyCap})` / `mcpserver.Register(*mcp.Server, *jobs.Registry)` signatures differ from the seam — reconcile by adjusting ONLY `internal/app/app.go`'s `newRegistryReal`/`registerReal` adapters (the contract types are fixed; the constructor shapes are the negotiated seam).

**Step Z7.4 — race + vet once more for confidence.**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go test -race ./internal/app/ ./cmd/pi-mcp/
```
Expected: `ok` for both (the app seam test is race-clean; no shared state).

**Commit:** `git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -am "Z7: integration green — go vet + go build + go test ./... (e2e skipped)"`

---

## Task Z8 — Install / registration (manual verification, documented in README/spec §13)

Not a unit test — these are operator steps verified by hand once the binary builds (Z7).

**Step Z8.1 — build to a PATH location.**
```
cd /root/pi-mcp && go build -o /usr/local/bin/pi-mcp ./cmd/pi-mcp
```
Expected: `/usr/local/bin/pi-mcp` exists and is executable.

**Step Z8.2 — register with Claude Code at user scope.**
```
claude mcp add -s user pi-mcp -- /usr/local/bin/pi-mcp
claude mcp list
```
Expected: `pi-mcp` appears in `claude mcp list` and reports connected (the go-sdk handshake succeeds over stdio). Claude Code inherits `AGENT_VAULT_*`/`HOME`/`PATH`; pi-mcp passes them to the grandchild `pi` via `cmd.Env = os.Environ()` (spec §13) — verified end-to-end by the Z6 e2e on a forked host.

**Step Z8.3 — smoke from the client side (optional, ties back to Z6).**
In a Claude Code session, confirm the 4 tools (`pi_workflow`, `pi_status`, `pi_list`, `pi_cancel`) are listed. A `pi_list{cwd:<a-project-with-runs>}` should return prior runs (reads `<cwd>/.pi/workflows/runs/*.json`).

**Verification gate (use `verification-before-completion` discipline):** do not claim "installed/working" until `claude mcp list` shows it connected AND either Z6 passed on a forked host OR `pi_list` returned real data. No green claims without command output.

**Commit (if any docs touched):** `git -C /root/pi-mcp commit -am "Z8: install + claude mcp add user-scope registration steps"`

---

## Sequencing & dependency summary
- Z1 → Z2 → Z3 establish the entrypoint + wiring seam (Z2/Z3 fully green only after packages B `jobs` + C `mcpserver` exist — integration gate).
- Z4, Z5 (Fase-0 fixtures) are **independent** and feed packages parser/runstore/jobs — do them early so those packages' tests can bind.
- Z6 (e2e) compiles after Z1-Z3 + SDK present; runs for real only on a fork-enabled host.
- Z7 is the cross-package binding gate (run after A/B/C merge).
- Z8 is operator install, last.

---
